<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async()=>{
  const canvas=document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle=document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel=document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveBtn=document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn=document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn=document.getElementById("viewBtn");
  const newBtn=document.getElementById("newBtn");
  const undoBtn=document.getElementById("undoBtn");
  const toast=document.getElementById("toast");
  let selectedCard=null;
  let undoStack=[];
  let currentLessonId=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") || sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") || "";

  const levelFromUrl=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl) lessonLevel.value=levelFromUrl;

  function showToast(text){toast.textContent=text;toast.classList.add("show");setTimeout(()=>toast.classList.remove("show"),1600)}
  function tick(){const t=document.getElementById("saveTick");t.classList.add("show");setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove("show"),1200)}
  function pushUndo(){undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);if(undoStack.length>50)undoStack.shift()}
  function clearEmpty(){const e=canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");if(e)e.remove()}
  function selectCard(card){selectedCard=card;document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(c=>c.classList.remove("active"));card.classList.add("active")}
  function bindCard(card){card.onclick=()=>selectCard(card);card.onfocus=()=>selectCard(card);card.oninput=()=>{}}
  function rebind(){document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(bindCard)}
  function addCard(html,editable=true){pushUndo();clearEmpty();const card=document.createElement("article");card.className="lesson-card";card.contentEditable=editable?"true":"false";card.innerHTML=html;bindCard(card);canvas.appendChild(card);selectCard(card);card.focus()}

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn=>{
    btn.onclick=()=>{
      const type=btn.dataset.block;
      if(type==="header")addCard("<h1>New Header</h1>");
      if(type==="subheader")addCard("<h2>New Sub Header</h2>");
      if(type==="outline")addCard("<h2>Lesson Outline</h2><ul><li>Warm-up</li><li>Main lesson</li><li>Practice</li><li>Review</li></ul>");
      if(type==="title")addCard("<h1>Lesson Title</h1><p>Add a short description of the lesson here.</p>");
      if(type==="objectives")addCard("<h2>Objectives</h2><p><strong>A la fin du cours, l’apprenant doit:</strong></p><ul><li>objectif 1</li><li>objectif 2</li><li>objectif 3</li></ul>");
      if(type==="text")addCard("<p>Write lesson content here...</p>");
      if(type==="image")document.getElementById("imageInput").click();
      if(type==="audio")document.getElementById("audioInput").click();
      if(type==="video")document.getElementById("videoInput").click();
    };
  });

  function apply(prop,val){if(!selectedCard){showToast("Select a lesson block first");return}selectedCard.style[prop]=val}
  document.getElementById("fontFamily").onchange=e=>apply("fontFamily",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("fontSize").onchange=e=>apply("fontSize",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("lineSpacing").onchange=e=>apply("lineHeight",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("letterSpacing").onchange=e=>apply("letterSpacing",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("alignment").onchange=e=>apply("textAlign",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("fontColor").oninput=e=>apply("color",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("backgroundColor").oninput=e=>apply("backgroundColor",e.target.value);

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-toggle]").forEach(btn=>{
    btn.onclick=()=>{
      if(!selectedCard){showToast("Select a lesson block first");return}
      const t=btn.dataset.toggle;
      if(t==="bold")selectedCard.style.fontWeight=selectedCard.style.fontWeight==="900"?"500":"900";
      if(t==="italic")selectedCard.style.fontStyle=selectedCard.style.fontStyle==="italic"?"normal":"italic";
      if(t==="underline")selectedCard.style.textDecoration=selectedCard.style.textDecoration==="underline"?"none":"underline";
    };
  });

  function readFile(file,cb){const r=new FileReader();r.onload=()=>cb(r.result);r.readAsDataURL(file)}
  document.getElementById("imageInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><img src="${src}" alt="Lesson image"></div>`,false));e.target.value=""};
  document.getElementById("audioInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`,false));e.target.value=""};
  document.getElementById("videoInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><video src="${src}" controls></video></div>`,false));e.target.value=""};

  undoBtn.onclick=()=>{if(!undoStack.length)return;canvas.innerHTML=undoStack.pop();rebind()};
  newBtn.onclick=()=>{currentLessonId="";sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");lessonTitle.value="";canvas.innerHTML='<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>';showToast("New lesson ready")};

  async function saveLesson(){
    const data={id:currentLessonId,title:lessonTitle.value.trim()||"Untitled Lesson Plan",name:lessonTitle.value.trim()||"Untitled Lesson Plan",level:lessonLevel.value,content:canvas.innerHTML,updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()};
    if(window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan){
      currentLessonId=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan(data);
    }else{
      currentLessonId=currentLessonId||("LP-"+Date.now());
      data.id=currentLessonId;
      const all=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans")||"[]");
      const i=all.findIndex(x=>x.id===currentLessonId);
      if(i>=0)all[i]=data;else all.push(data);
      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans",JSON.stringify(all));
    }
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",currentLessonId);
    tick();showToast("Saved");
  }

  saveBtn.onclick=saveLesson;
  editBtn.onclick=async()=>{location.href="/teacher/lesson-plans.html"};
  viewBtn.onclick=async()=>{await saveLesson();window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId),"_blank")};

  const template=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan")||"{}");
  if(template && template.type==="template"){
    lessonTitle.value=template.title||"";
    lessonLevel.value=template.level||lessonLevel.value;
    canvas.innerHTML=`
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><h2>${template.title||"Lesson Template"}</h2><p><strong>Objective:</strong> ${template.objective||""}</p></article>
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><p><strong>Lesson Flow:</strong> ${template.flow||""}</p></article>
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><p><strong>Materials:</strong> ${template.materials||""}</p></article>`;
    rebind();
  }else if(currentLessonId && window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan){
    const plan=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);
    if(plan){lessonTitle.value=plan.title||plan.name||"";lessonLevel.value=plan.level||lessonLevel.value;canvas.innerHTML=plan.content||canvas.innerHTML;rebind()}
  }
});
</script>

<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_AUTOSAVE_AND_DELETE">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveTick = document.getElementById("saveTick");

  let autosaveTimer = null;

  function showSaving(){
    if(!saveTick) return;
    saveTick.textContent = "Saving...";
    saveTick.style.opacity = "1";
    saveTick.classList.add("show");
  }

  function showSaved(){
    if(!saveTick) return;
    saveTick.textContent = "Saved ✓";
    saveTick.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => {
      saveTick.classList.remove("show");
      saveTick.textContent = "✓";
    }, 1400);
  }

  async function autoSave(){
    if(!canvas) return;
    showSaving();

    const existingId =
      window.currentLessonId ||
      sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") ||
      "";

    const data = {
      id: existingId,
      title: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      name: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      level: levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner",
      content: canvas.innerHTML || "",
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };

    try{
      if(window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan){
        const id = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan(data);
        window.currentLessonId = id;
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
      }else{
        const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");
        const id = data.id || ("LP-" + Date.now());
        data.id = id;

        const i = all.findIndex(x => x.id === id);
        if(i >= 0) all[i] = data;
        else all.push(data);

        localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(all));
        window.currentLessonId = id;
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
      }

      showSaved();
    }catch(err){
      console.error("Autosave error:", err);
      if(saveTick){
        saveTick.textContent = "Not saved";
        saveTick.classList.add("show");
      }
    }
  }

  function triggerAutoSave(){
    clearTimeout(autosaveTimer);
    autosaveTimer = setTimeout(autoSave, 900);
  }

  function attachDeleteButtons(){
    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(card => {
      if(card.querySelector(".lesson-block-delete")) return;

      card.style.position = "relative";

      const btn = document.createElement("button");
      btn.className = "lesson-block-delete";
      btn.type = "button";
      btn.textContent = "×";
      btn.title = "Delete block";

      btn.onclick = e => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        card.style.transition = "transform .18s ease, opacity .18s ease";
        card.style.transform = "scale(.96)";
        card.style.opacity = "0";

        setTimeout(() => {
          card.remove();
          triggerAutoSave();
        }, 180);
      };

      card.appendChild(btn);
    });
  }

  if(canvas){
    canvas.addEventListener("input", triggerAutoSave);
    canvas.addEventListener("change", triggerAutoSave);

    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => attachDeleteButtons());
    observer.observe(canvas, { childList:true, subtree:false });

    attachDeleteButtons();
  }

  titleInput?.addEventListener("input", triggerAutoSave);
  levelInput?.addEventListener("change", triggerAutoSave);
});
</script>

<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_LOAD_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {

  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");

  let lessonId =
    new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") ||
    sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId");

  // =========================
  // LOAD FROM FIREBASE
  // =========================
  async function loadFromFirebase(id){
    if(!window.ImpactFirebaseStore || !window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan) return null;
    try{
      return await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(id);
    }catch(e){
      console.warn("Firebase load failed", e);
      return null;
    }
  }

  // =========================
  // LOAD FROM LOCAL STORAGE
  // =========================
  function loadFromLocal(id){
    const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");
    return all.find(x => x.id === id);
  }

  // =========================
  // APPLY LESSON TO UI
  // =========================
  function applyLesson(data){
    if(!data) return;

    if(titleInput) titleInput.value = data.title || data.name || "";
    if(levelInput) levelInput.value = data.level || "Absolute Beginner";
    if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = data.content || "";

    window.currentLessonId = data.id;
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", data.id);
  }

  // =========================
  // LOAD FLOW
  // =========================
  if(lessonId){

    let lesson = await loadFromFirebase(lessonId);

    if(!lesson){
      lesson = loadFromLocal(lessonId);
    }

    if(lesson){
      applyLesson(lesson);
    }

  } else {

    // Load LAST SAVED automatically
    const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

    if(all.length){
      const latest = all.sort((a,b)=> new Date(b.updatedAt) - new Date(a.updatedAt))[0];
      applyLesson(latest);
    }
  }

});
</script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_DELETE_FINAL_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");

  function addDeleteButtons(){
    if(!canvas) return;

    canvas.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(card => {
      if(card.querySelector(".lesson-block-delete")) return;

      card.style.position = "relative";

      const btn = document.createElement("button");
      btn.className = "lesson-block-delete";
      btn.type = "button";
      btn.textContent = "×";
      btn.setAttribute("contenteditable","false");

      btn.addEventListener("mousedown", e => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
      });

      btn.addEventListener("click", e => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        card.remove();

        setTimeout(() => {
          if(saveBtn) saveBtn.click();
        }, 150);
      });

      card.appendChild(btn);
    });
  }

  addDeleteButtons();

  const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
    setTimeout(addDeleteButtons, 50);
  });

  if(canvas){
    observer.observe(canvas, {
      childList:true,
      subtree:true
    });
  }

  setTimeout(addDeleteButtons, 500);
  setTimeout(addDeleteButtons, 1500);
});
</script>

<script id="lesson-builder-stability-fix">

(function(){

let autosaveTimer = null;
const AUTOSAVE_DELAY = 3000;

function scheduleAutosave(){

  clearTimeout(autosaveTimer);

  autosaveTimer = setTimeout(() => {

    const saveBtn =
      document.querySelector("#saveBtn") ||
      [...document.querySelectorAll("button")]
      .find(btn => btn.textContent.trim().toLowerCase() === "save");

    if(saveBtn){
      saveBtn.click();
    }

  }, AUTOSAVE_DELAY);
}

document.addEventListener("input", scheduleAutosave);

document.querySelectorAll("img,video").forEach(media => {

  if(media.closest(".resize-wrap")) return;

  const wrap = document.createElement("div");

  wrap.className = "resize-wrap";

  wrap.style.width = "70%";
  wrap.style.maxWidth = "100%";
  wrap.style.resize = "both";
  wrap.style.overflow = "auto";
  wrap.style.display = "inline-block";
  wrap.style.borderRadius = "18px";
  wrap.style.padding = "8px";
  wrap.style.border = "1px dashed rgba(255,255,255,.18)";

  media.parentNode.insertBefore(wrap, media);

  wrap.appendChild(media);

  media.style.width = "100%";
  media.style.height = "auto";
  media.style.display = "block";
});

document.querySelectorAll("button").forEach(btn => {

  const txt = btn.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();

  if(txt.includes("align left")){

    btn.onclick = () => {
      document.querySelectorAll(".resize-wrap").forEach(el=>{
        el.style.marginLeft = "0";
        el.style.marginRight = "auto";
      });
    };
  }

  if(txt.includes("align center")){

    btn.onclick = () => {
      document.querySelectorAll(".resize-wrap").forEach(el=>{
        el.style.marginLeft = "auto";
        el.style.marginRight = "auto";
      });
    };
  }

  if(txt.includes("align right")){

    btn.onclick = () => {
      document.querySelectorAll(".resize-wrap").forEach(el=>{
        el.style.marginLeft = "auto";
        el.style.marginRight = "0";
      });
    };
  }

});

const viewBtn =
  document.querySelector("#viewBtn") ||
  [...document.querySelectorAll("button")]
  .find(btn => btn.textContent.trim().toLowerCase() === "view");

if(viewBtn){

  viewBtn.onclick = function(e){

    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();

    const canvas =
      document.querySelector(".lesson-canvas") ||
      document.querySelector("#canvas");

    if(!canvas){
      alert("No lesson canvas found.");
      return;
    }

    const cleanHTML = canvas.innerHTML;

    const win = window.open("", "_blank");

    win.document.write(`
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<title>Lesson View</title>

<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;600;700;800&family=Sorts+Mill+Goudy&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">

<style>

body{
  background:#0b1020;
  color:white;
  font-family:Inter,sans-serif;
  margin:0;
}

main{
  width:min(900px,92vw);
  margin:auto;
  padding:60px 0 100px;
  line-height:1.8;
}

img,video{
  max-width:100%;
  border-radius:18px;
  margin:16px 0;
}

.lesson-card,
.card,
.block{
  background:transparent !important;
  border:none !important;
  box-shadow:none !important;
  padding:0 !important;
  margin:0 0 20px !important;
}

</style>
</head>

<body>
<main>
${cleanHTML}
</main>
</body>
</html>
`);

    win.document.close();
  };
}

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async()=>{
  const canvas=document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle=document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel=document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveBtn=document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn=document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn=document.getElementById("viewBtn");
  const newBtn=document.getElementById("newBtn");
  const undoBtn=document.getElementById("undoBtn");
  const toast=document.getElementById("toast");
  let selectedCard=null;
  let undoStack=[];
  let currentLessonId=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") || sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") || "";

  const levelFromUrl=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl) lessonLevel.value=levelFromUrl;

  function showToast(text){toast.textContent=text;toast.classList.add("show");setTimeout(()=>toast.classList.remove("show"),1600)}
  function tick(){const t=document.getElementById("saveTick");t.classList.add("show");setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove("show"),1200)}
  function pushUndo(){undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);if(undoStack.length>50)undoStack.shift()}
  function clearEmpty(){const e=canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");if(e)e.remove()}
  function selectCard(card){selectedCard=card;document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(c=>c.classList.remove("active"));card.classList.add("active")}
  function bindCard(card){card.onclick=()=>selectCard(card);card.onfocus=()=>selectCard(card);card.oninput=()=>{}}
  function rebind(){document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(bindCard)}
  function addCard(html,editable=true){pushUndo();clearEmpty();const card=document.createElement("article");card.className="lesson-card";card.contentEditable=editable?"true":"false";card.innerHTML=html;bindCard(card);canvas.appendChild(card);selectCard(card);card.focus()}

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn=>{
    btn.onclick=()=>{
      const type=btn.dataset.block;
      if(type==="header")addCard("<h1>New Header</h1>");
      if(type==="subheader")addCard("<h2>New Sub Header</h2>");
      if(type==="outline")addCard("<h2>Lesson Outline</h2><ul><li>Warm-up</li><li>Main lesson</li><li>Practice</li><li>Review</li></ul>");
      if(type==="title")addCard("<h1>Lesson Title</h1><p>Add a short description of the lesson here.</p>");
      if(type==="objectives")addCard("<h2>Objectives</h2><p><strong>A la fin du cours, l’apprenant doit:</strong></p><ul><li>objectif 1</li><li>objectif 2</li><li>objectif 3</li></ul>");
      if(type==="text")addCard("<p>Write lesson content here...</p>");
      if(type==="image")document.getElementById("imageInput").click();
      if(type==="audio")document.getElementById("audioInput").click();
      if(type==="video")document.getElementById("videoInput").click();
    };
  });

  function apply(prop,val){if(!selectedCard){showToast("Select a lesson block first");return}selectedCard.style[prop]=val}
  document.getElementById("fontFamily").onchange=e=>apply("fontFamily",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("fontSize").onchange=e=>apply("fontSize",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("lineSpacing").onchange=e=>apply("lineHeight",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("letterSpacing").onchange=e=>apply("letterSpacing",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("alignment").onchange=e=>apply("textAlign",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("fontColor").oninput=e=>apply("color",e.target.value);
  document.getElementById("backgroundColor").oninput=e=>apply("backgroundColor",e.target.value);

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-toggle]").forEach(btn=>{
    btn.onclick=()=>{
      if(!selectedCard){showToast("Select a lesson block first");return}
      const t=btn.dataset.toggle;
      if(t==="bold")selectedCard.style.fontWeight=selectedCard.style.fontWeight==="900"?"500":"900";
      if(t==="italic")selectedCard.style.fontStyle=selectedCard.style.fontStyle==="italic"?"normal":"italic";
      if(t==="underline")selectedCard.style.textDecoration=selectedCard.style.textDecoration==="underline"?"none":"underline";
    };
  });

  function readFile(file,cb){const r=new FileReader();r.onload=()=>cb(r.result);r.readAsDataURL(file)}
  document.getElementById("imageInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><img src="${src}" alt="Lesson image"></div>`,false));e.target.value=""};
  document.getElementById("audioInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`,false));e.target.value=""};
  document.getElementById("videoInput").onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)readFile(f,src=>addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><video src="${src}" controls></video></div>`,false));e.target.value=""};

  undoBtn.onclick=()=>{if(!undoStack.length)return;canvas.innerHTML=undoStack.pop();rebind()};
  newBtn.onclick=()=>{currentLessonId="";sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");lessonTitle.value="";canvas.innerHTML='<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>';showToast("New lesson ready")};

  async function saveLesson(){
    const data={id:currentLessonId,title:lessonTitle.value.trim()||"Untitled Lesson Plan",name:lessonTitle.value.trim()||"Untitled Lesson Plan",level:lessonLevel.value,content:canvas.innerHTML,updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()};
    if(window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan){
      currentLessonId=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan(data);
    }else{
      currentLessonId=currentLessonId||("LP-"+Date.now());
      data.id=currentLessonId;
      const all=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans")||"[]");
      const i=all.findIndex(x=>x.id===currentLessonId);
      if(i>=0)all[i]=data;else all.push(data);
      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans",JSON.stringify(all));
    }
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",currentLessonId);
    tick();showToast("Saved");
  }

  saveBtn.onclick=saveLesson;
  editBtn.onclick=async()=>{location.href="/teacher/lesson-plans.html"};
  viewBtn.onclick=async()=>{await saveLesson();window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId),"_blank")};

  const template=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan")||"{}");
  if(template && template.type==="template"){
    lessonTitle.value=template.title||"";
    lessonLevel.value=template.level||lessonLevel.value;
    canvas.innerHTML=`
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><h2>${template.title||"Lesson Template"}</h2><p><strong>Objective:</strong> ${template.objective||""}</p></article>
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><p><strong>Lesson Flow:</strong> ${template.flow||""}</p></article>
      <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true"><p><strong>Materials:</strong> ${template.materials||""}</p></article>`;
    rebind();
  }else if(currentLessonId && window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan){
    const plan=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);
    if(plan){lessonTitle.value=plan.title||plan.name||"";lessonLevel.value=plan.level||lessonLevel.value;canvas.innerHTML=plan.content||canvas.innerHTML;rebind()}
  }
});
</script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_AUTOSAVE_AND_DELETE">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveTick = document.getElementById("saveTick");

  let autosaveTimer = null;

  function showSaving(){
    if(!saveTick) return;
    saveTick.textContent = "Saving...";
    saveTick.style.opacity = "1";
    saveTick.classList.add("show");
  }

  function showSaved(){
    if(!saveTick) return;
    saveTick.textContent = "Saved ✓";
    saveTick.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => {
      saveTick.classList.remove("show");
      saveTick.textContent = "✓";
    }, 1400);
  }

  async function autoSave(){
    if(!canvas) return;
    showSaving();

    const existingId =
      window.currentLessonId ||
      sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") ||
      "";

    const data = {
      id: existingId,
      title: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      name: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      level: levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner",
      content: canvas.innerHTML || "",
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };

    try{
      if(window.ImpactFirebaseStore && window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan){
        const id = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan(data);
        window.currentLessonId = id;
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
      }else{
        const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");
        const id = data.id || ("LP-" + Date.now());
        data.id = id;

        const i = all.findIndex(x => x.id === id);
        if(i >= 0) all[i] = data;
        else all.push(data);

        localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(all));
        window.currentLessonId = id;
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
      }

      showSaved();
    }catch(err){
      console.error("Autosave error:", err);
      if(saveTick){
        saveTick.textContent = "Not saved";
        saveTick.classList.add("show");
      }
    }
  }

  function triggerAutoSave(){
    clearTimeout(autosaveTimer);
    autosaveTimer = setTimeout(autoSave, 900);
  }

  function attachDeleteButtons(){
    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(card => {
      if(card.querySelector(".lesson-block-delete")) return;

      card.style.position = "relative";

      const btn = document.createElement("button");
      btn.className = "lesson-block-delete";
      btn.type = "button";
      btn.textContent = "×";
      btn.title = "Delete block";

      btn.onclick = e => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        card.style.transition = "transform .18s ease, opacity .18s ease";
        card.style.transform = "scale(.96)";
        card.style.opacity = "0";

        setTimeout(() => {
          card.remove();
          triggerAutoSave();
        }, 180);
      };

      card.appendChild(btn);
    });
  }

  if(canvas){
    canvas.addEventListener("input", triggerAutoSave);
    canvas.addEventListener("change", triggerAutoSave);

    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => attachDeleteButtons());
    observer.observe(canvas, { childList:true, subtree:false });

    attachDeleteButtons();
  }

  titleInput?.addEventListener("input", triggerAutoSave);
  levelInput?.addEventListener("change", triggerAutoSave);
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="/js/impact-global-bg.js?v=lesson-builder-final-003"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-page-nav.js?v=lesson-builder-final-003"></script>

<script>
(function(){
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");

  let selectedCard = null;
  let currentId = null;

  const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
  const initialLevel = params.get("level") || sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel");
  if(initialLevel) lessonLevel.value = initialLevel;

  function getPlans(){
    try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");}
    catch(e){return [];}
  }

  function setPlans(list){
    localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(list));
  }

  function uid(){
    return "LP-" + Date.now().toString(36).toUpperCase();
  }

  let undoStack = [];
  let undoTimer = null;

  function pushUndo(){
    undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);
    if(undoStack.length > 40) undoStack.shift();
  }

  function pushUndoDebounced(){
    clearTimeout(undoTimer);
    undoTimer = setTimeout(pushUndo, 400);
  }

  function undoCanvas(){
    if(!undoStack.length) return;
    const previous = undoStack.pop();
    canvas.innerHTML = previous;
    rebindCanvasCards();
  }

  function rebindCanvasCards(){
    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(card => {
      card.addEventListener("click", () => selectCard(card));
      card.addEventListener("focus", () => selectCard(card));
      card.addEventListener("input", pushUndoDebounced);
    });
  }

  function resetToolbarDefaults(){
    const fontFamily = document.getElementById("fontFamily");
    const fontSize = document.getElementById("fontSize");
    const lineSpacing = document.getElementById("lineSpacing");
    const letterSpacing = document.getElementById("letterSpacing");
    const alignment = document.getElementById("alignment");
    const fontColor = document.getElementById("fontColor");
    const backgroundColor = document.getElementById("backgroundColor");

    if(fontFamily) fontFamily.value = "Inter";
    if(fontSize) fontSize.value = "16px";
    if(lineSpacing) lineSpacing.value = "1.5";
    if(letterSpacing) letterSpacing.value = "0px";
    if(alignment) alignment.value = "left";
    if(fontColor) fontColor.value = "#ffffff";
    if(backgroundColor) backgroundColor.value = "#24304f";
  }

  function showFileHint(text){
    const hint = document.getElementById("fileHint");
    if(!hint) return;
    hint.textContent = text;
    hint.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => hint.classList.remove("show"), 1800);
  }

  function clearEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function selectCard(card){
    selectedCard = card;
    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(c => c.classList.remove("active"));
    card.classList.add("active");
  }

  function addCard(type, innerHtml){
    pushUndo();
    resetToolbarDefaults();
    clearEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "true";
    card.dataset.blockType = type;
    card.innerHTML = innerHtml.replace(/<div class="lesson-label">[\s\S]*?<\/div>/g, "");

    card.style.fontFamily = "Inter";
    card.style.fontSize = "16px";
    card.style.lineHeight = "1.5";
    card.style.letterSpacing = "0px";
    card.style.textAlign = "left";
    card.style.color = "#ffffff";
    card.style.backgroundColor = "";

    card.addEventListener("click", () => selectCard(card));
    card.addEventListener("focus", () => selectCard(card));
    card.addEventListener("input", pushUndoDebounced);

    canvas.appendChild(card);
    selectCard(card);
    card.focus();
  }

  function blockTemplate(type){
    const label = '';

    if(type === "header"){
      return label + '<h1>New Header</h1>';
    }

    if(type === "subheader"){
      return label + '<h2>New Sub Header</h2>';
    }

    if(type === "outline"){
      return label + '<h2>Lesson Outline</h2><ul><li>Warm-up</li><li>Main lesson</li><li>Practice</li><li>Review</li></ul>';
    }

    if(type === "title"){
      return label + '<h1>Lesson Title</h1><p>Add a short description of the lesson here.</p>';
    }

    if(type === "objectives"){
      return label + '<h2>Objectives</h2><p><strong>A la fin du cours, l’apprenant doit:</strong></p><ul><li>objectif 1</li><li>objectif 2</li><li>objectif 3</li></ul>';
    }

    if(type === "text"){
      return label + '<p>Write lesson content here...</p>';
    }

    if(type === "image"){
        showFileHint("Choose image source");
        document.getElementById("imageChoiceModal").classList.add("show");
        return;
      }

      if(type === "audio"){
        showFileHint("Select an audio file from your device");
        document.getElementById("audioInput").click();
        return;
      }

      if(type === "video"){
        showFileHint("Select a video file from your device");
        document.getElementById("videoInput").click();
        return;
      }

      addCard(type, blockTemplate(type));
    });
  });

  function apply(prop, value){
    if(!selectedCard){
      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
      return;
    }
    selectedCard.style[prop] = value;
  }

  document.getElementById("fontFamily").addEventListener("change", e => apply("fontFamily", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("fontSize").addEventListener("change", e => apply("fontSize", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("lineSpacing").addEventListener("change", e => apply("lineHeight", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("letterSpacing").addEventListener("change", e => apply("letterSpacing", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("alignment").addEventListener("change", e => apply("textAlign", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("fontColor").addEventListener("input", e => apply("color", e.target.value));
  document.getElementById("backgroundColor").addEventListener("input", e => apply("backgroundColor", e.target.value));

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-toggle]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      if(!selectedCard){
        const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
        return;
      }

      const t = btn.dataset.toggle;
      if(t === "bold") selectedCard.style.fontWeight = selectedCard.style.fontWeight === "900" ? "700" : "900";
      if(t === "italic") selectedCard.style.fontStyle = selectedCard.style.fontStyle === "italic" ? "normal" : "italic";
      if(t === "underline") selectedCard.style.textDecoration = selectedCard.style.textDecoration === "underline" ? "none" : "underline";
    });
  });

  document.getElementById("imageDeviceBtn").onclick = () => {
    document.getElementById("imageChoiceModal").classList.remove("show");
    document.getElementById("imageInput").click();
  };

  document.getElementById("imageGoogleBtn").onclick = () => {
    const q = prompt("Search Google Images for:");
    if(q) window.open("https://www.google.com/search?tbm=isch&q=" + encodeURIComponent(q), "_blank");
  };

  document.getElementById("imageStockBtn").onclick = () => {
    const q = prompt("Search stock photos for:");
    if(q) window.open("https://unsplash.com/s/photos/" + encodeURIComponent(q), "_blank");
  };

  document.getElementById("closeImageChoiceBtn").onclick = () => {
    document.getElementById("imageChoiceModal").classList.remove("show");
  };

  function fileToDataUrl(file, cb){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => cb(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  document.getElementById("imageInput").addEventListener("change", e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if(file) fileToDataUrl(file, src => addCard("image", '<div class="lesson-label">Image Resource</div><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div>'));
    e.target.value = "";
  });

  document.getElementById("audioInput").addEventListener("change", e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if(file) fileToDataUrl(file, src => addCard("audio", '<div class="lesson-label">Audio Resource</div><audio src="'+src+'" controls></audio>'));
    e.target.value = "";
  });

  document.getElementById("videoInput").addEventListener("change", e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if(file) fileToDataUrl(file, src => addCard("video", '<div class="lesson-label">Video Resource</div><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video>'));
    e.target.value = "";
  });

  document.getElementById("undoBtn").onclick = undoCanvas; document.getElementById("newBtn").onclick = () => {
    if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
    currentId = null;
    selectedCard = null; resetToolbarDefaults(); lessonTitle.value = "";
    canvas.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>';
  };

  document.getElementById("saveBtn").onclick = () => {
    const title = lessonTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
    const level = lessonLevel.value;

    if(!currentId) currentId = uid();

    const record = {
      id: currentId,
      title,
      name: title,
      level,
      content: canvas.innerHTML,
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    };

    const list = getPlans();
    const index = list.findIndex(p => p.id === currentId);
    if(index >= 0) list[index] = record;
    else list.push(record);

    setPlans(list);
    const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
  };

  function renderEditFiles(){
    const level = document.getElementById("editLevelSelect").value;
    const files = getPlans().filter(p => p.level === level);
    const box = document.getElementById("editFileList");

    box.innerHTML = files.length
      ? files.map(p => '<button class="file-btn" data-id="'+p.id+'" type="button">'+p.title+'</button>').join("")
      : '<p style="color:rgba(255,255,255,.75);font-weight:800;">No files in this folder yet.</p>';

    box.querySelectorAll(".file-btn").forEach(btn => {
      btn.onclick = () => {
        const file = getPlans().find(p => p.id === btn.dataset.id);
        if(!file) return;
        currentId = file.id;
        lessonTitle.value = file.title || file.name || "";
        lessonLevel.value = file.level || "Absolute Beginner";
        canvas.innerHTML = file.content || ""; rebindCanvasCards(); rebindCanvasCards();
        document.getElementById("editModal").classList.remove("show");
      };
    });
  }

  document.getElementById("editBtn").onclick = () => {
    document.getElementById("editLevelSelect").value = lessonLevel.value;
    renderEditFiles();
    document.getElementById("editModal").classList.add("show");
  };

  document.getElementById("editLevelSelect").addEventListener("change", renderEditFiles);
  document.getElementById("closeEditBtn").onclick = () => document.getElementById("editModal").classList.remove("show");

  document.getElementById("viewBtn").onclick = () => {
    const title = lessonTitle.value || "Lesson Plan";
    const clean = canvas.innerHTML
      .replace(/contenteditable="true"/g, "")
      .replace(/class="lesson-card active"/g, "")
      .replace(/class="lesson-card"/g, "")
      .replace(/<article\s*>/g, "<section>")
      .replace(/<\/article>/g, "</section>");

    const w = window.open("", "_blank");
    w.document.write(`
      <!DOCTYPE html>
      <html>
      <head>
        <meta charset="UTF-8">
        <title>${title}</title>
        <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Sorts+Mill+Goudy&family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700;800;900&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
        <style>
          body{
            margin:0;
            min-height:100vh;
            background:
              radial-gradient(circle at 50% 10%, rgba(255,255,255,.08), transparent 28%),
              linear-gradient(180deg,#111827,#05060b);
            color:#f8fafc;
          }
          .doc{
            max-width:900px;
            margin:0 auto;
            padding:70px 42px;
            font-family:Inter,system-ui,sans-serif;
            line-height:1.75;
          }
          h1,h2,h3{
            font-family:"Sorts Mill Goudy",Georgia,serif;
            font-weight:400;
            margin:24px 0 12px;
          }
          h1{font-size:3rem}
          h2{font-size:2.1rem}
          h3{font-size:1.55rem}
          p{margin:10px 0}
          ul{margin:10px 0 18px 26px}

      <script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {

  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");

  function addCard(html){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "true";
    card.innerHTML = html;

    canvas.appendChild(card);
    card.focus();
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.onclick = () => {
      const type = btn.getAttribute("data-block");

      btn.style.transform = "scale(.95)";
      setTimeout(() => btn.style.transform = "", 120);

      if(type === "header"){
        addCard("<h1>New Header</h1>");
      }

      if(type === "subheader"){
        addCard("<h2>New Sub Header</h2>");
      }

      if(type === "outline"){
        addCard("<h2>Lesson Outline</h2><ul><li>Warm-up</li><li>Main lesson</li><li>Practice</li></ul>");
      }

      if(type === "title"){
        addCard("<h1>Lesson Title</h1><p>Description...</p>");
      }

      if(type === "objectives"){
        addCard("<h2>Objectives</h2><p><strong>A la fin du cours, l’apprenant doit:</strong></p><ul><li>...</li></ul>");
      }

      if(type === "text"){
        addCard("<p>Write lesson content here...</p>");
      }

      if(type === "image"){
        document.getElementById("imageInput").click();
      }

      if(type === "audio"){
        document.getElementById("audioInput").click();
      }

      if(type === "video"){
        document.getElementById("videoInput").click();
      }
    };
  });

});
</script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_MEDIA_AND_SETTINGS_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function addCard(html){
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "true";
    card.innerHTML = html;

    canvas.appendChild(card);
    card.focus();
  }

  function fileToDataUrl(file, callback){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => callback(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  const newBtn = document.getElementById("newBtn");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn = document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn = document.getElementById("viewBtn");

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      lessonTitle.value = "";
      canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
      const level = lessonLevel.value || "Absolute Beginner";

      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

      const record = {
        id: "LP-" + Date.now(),
        title,
        name: title,
        level,
        content: canvas.innerHTML,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };

      saved.push(record);
      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(saved));

      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = () => {
      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");
      const level = lessonLevel.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const files = saved.filter(item => item.level === level);

      if(!files.length){
        const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
        return;
      }

      const list = files.map((item, index) => `${index + 1}. ${item.title || item.name}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);

      const selected = files[Number(choice) - 1];
      if(!selected) return;

      lessonTitle.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle.value.trim() || "Lesson Plan";
      const content = canvas.innerHTML
        .replaceAll('contenteditable="true"', '')
        .replaceAll('class="lesson-card active"', '')
        .replaceAll('class="lesson-card"', '');

      const w = window.open("", "_blank");
      w.document.write(`
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head>
          <meta charset="UTF-8">
          <title>${title}</title>
          <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Sorts+Mill+Goudy&family=Inter:wght@300;400;600;800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
          <style>
            body{
              margin:0;
              background:linear-gradient(180deg,#111827,#05060b);
              color:#f8fafc;
              font-family:Inter,system-ui,sans-serif;
            }
            main{
              max-width:900px;
              margin:0 auto;
              padding:70px 42px;
              line-height:1.75;
            }
            h1,h2,h3{
              font-family:"Sorts Mill Goudy",Georgia,serif;
              font-weight:400;
            }
            img,video{
              max-width:100%;
              border-radius:18px;
              display:block;
              margin:18px 0;
            }
            audio{
              width:100%;
              margin:18px 0;
            }
          /* RESIZABLE LESSON MEDIA */
.lesson-media-wrap{
  display:inline-block;
  max-width:100%;
  resize:both;
  overflow:auto;
  min-width:160px;
  min-height:100px;
  padding:8px;
  border-radius:18px;
  border:1px dashed rgba(232,216,166,.35);
}

.lesson-media-wrap img,
.lesson-media-wrap video{
  width:100%;
  height:auto;
  display:block;
  border-radius:14px;
}

  color:#fff;

        <script id="LESSON_BUILDER_RESIZE_SAVE_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function fileToDataUrl(file, cb){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => cb(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  function showSaveToast(level){
    const toast = document.getElementById("saveToast");
    if(!toast) return;
    toast.textContent = "Saved to " + level + " folder";
    toast.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove("show"), 2200);
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
      const level = lessonLevel?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const content = canvas?.innerHTML || "";

      const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

      const existingId = saveBtn.dataset.currentId || "";
      const id = existingId || ("LP-" + Date.now());

      const record = {
        id,
        title,
        name:title,
        level,
        content,
        updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
      };

      const index = all.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
      if(index >= 0) all[index] = record;
      else all.push(record);

      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(all));
      saveBtn.dataset.currentId = id;

      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
    };
  }
});
</script>
<script id="FINAL_IMAGE_UNDO_REPAIR">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const undoBtn = document.getElementById("undoBtn");

  let undoStack = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function saveUndo(){
    undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);
    if(undoStack.length > 50) undoStack.shift();
  }

  function readFile(file, callback){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => callback(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    saveUndo();
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <img src="${src}" alt="Lesson image">
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <video src="${src}" controls></video>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <audio src="${src}" controls></audio>
      `;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const type = btn.dataset.block;
      if(!["image","audio","video"].includes(type)){
        saveUndo();
      }
    }, true);
  });

  if(undoBtn){
    undoBtn.textContent = "↶";
    undoBtn.title = "Undo";
    undoBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!undoStack.length) return;
      canvas.innerHTML = undoStack.pop();
    };
  }
});
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-storage-final-001"></script>

<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>

<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_FIREBASE_FINAL">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn = document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn = document.getElementById("viewBtn");
  const newBtn = document.getElementById("newBtn");

  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");

  let currentLessonId =
    new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") ||
    sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") ||
    "";

  let mediaList = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function savedTick(){
    const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
    if(tick){
      tick.classList.add("show");
      setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
    }
  }

  function addMediaCard(media){
    removeEmpty();
    mediaList.push(media);

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card lesson-media-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";
    card.dataset.storagePath = media.path || "";
    card.dataset.mediaUrl = media.url || "";

    if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("image")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><img src="${media.url}" alt="${media.name || "Lesson image"}"></div>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("audio")){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${media.url}" controls></audio>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("video")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><video src="${media.url}" controls></video></div>`;
    } else {
      card.innerHTML = `<a href="${media.url}" target="_blank">${media.name || "Uploaded file"}</a>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  async function bindUpload(input, folder){
    if(!input) return;

    input.onchange = async (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const lessonTitle = titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson";
      const subfolder = level + "/" + lessonTitle;

      const media = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.uploadFile(file, folder, subfolder);
      addMediaCard(media);

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  await bindUpload(imageInput, "lesson-images");
  await bindUpload(audioInput, "lesson-audio");
  await bindUpload(videoInput, "lesson-video");

  async function saveLesson(){
    const id = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan({
      id: currentLessonId,
      title: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      level: levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner",
      content: canvas?.innerHTML || "",
      media: mediaList
    });

    currentLessonId = id;
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
    savedTick();
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = saveLesson;
  }

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      currentLessonId = "";
      mediaList = [];
      sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = "";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = async () => {
      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const plans = (await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()).filter(p => p.level === level);

      if(!plans.length){
        alert("No saved lesson plans in this level folder yet.");
        return;
      }

      const list = plans.map((p,i)=>`${i+1}. ${p.title || p.name || "Untitled Lesson"}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);
      const selected = plans[Number(choice)-1];

      if(!selected) return;

      currentLessonId = selected.id;
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", currentLessonId);

      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = async () => {
      await saveLesson();
      window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id=" + encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId), "_blank");
    };
  }

  const levelFromUrl = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl && levelInput){
    levelInput.value = levelFromUrl;
  }

  if(currentLessonId){
    const selected = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);

    if(selected){
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    }
  }
});
</script>

<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_RESIZE_SAVE_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function fileToDataUrl(file, cb){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => cb(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  function showSaveToast(level){
    const toast = document.getElementById("saveToast");
    if(!toast) return;
    toast.textContent = "Saved to " + level + " folder";
    toast.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove("show"), 2200);
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
      const level = lessonLevel?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const content = canvas?.innerHTML || "";

      const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

      const existingId = saveBtn.dataset.currentId || "";
      const id = existingId || ("LP-" + Date.now());

      const record = {
        id,
        title,
        name:title,
        level,
        content,
        updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
      };

      const index = all.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
      if(index >= 0) all[index] = record;
      else all.push(record);

      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(all));
      saveBtn.dataset.currentId = id;

      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
    };
  }
});
</script>
<script id="FINAL_IMAGE_UNDO_REPAIR">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const undoBtn = document.getElementById("undoBtn");

  let undoStack = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function saveUndo(){
    undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);
    if(undoStack.length > 50) undoStack.shift();
  }

  function readFile(file, callback){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => callback(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    saveUndo();
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <img src="${src}" alt="Lesson image">
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <video src="${src}" controls></video>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <audio src="${src}" controls></audio>
      `;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const type = btn.dataset.block;
      if(!["image","audio","video"].includes(type)){
        saveUndo();
      }
    }, true);
  });

  if(undoBtn){
    undoBtn.textContent = "↶";
    undoBtn.title = "Undo";
    undoBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!undoStack.length) return;
      canvas.innerHTML = undoStack.pop();
    };
  }
});
</script>

<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>

<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_FIREBASE_FINAL">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn = document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn = document.getElementById("viewBtn");
  const newBtn = document.getElementById("newBtn");

  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");

  let currentLessonId =
    new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") ||
    sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") ||
    "";

  let mediaList = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function savedTick(){
    const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
    if(tick){
      tick.classList.add("show");
      setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
    }
  }

  function addMediaCard(media){
    removeEmpty();
    mediaList.push(media);

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card lesson-media-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";
    card.dataset.storagePath = media.path || "";
    card.dataset.mediaUrl = media.url || "";

    if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("image")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><img src="${media.url}" alt="${media.name || "Lesson image"}"></div>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("audio")){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${media.url}" controls></audio>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("video")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><video src="${media.url}" controls></video></div>`;
    } else {
      card.innerHTML = `<a href="${media.url}" target="_blank">${media.name || "Uploaded file"}</a>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  async function bindUpload(input, folder){
    if(!input) return;

    input.onchange = async (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const lessonTitle = titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson";
      const subfolder = level + "/" + lessonTitle;

      const media = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.uploadFile(file, folder, subfolder);
      addMediaCard(media);

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  await bindUpload(imageInput, "lesson-images");
  await bindUpload(audioInput, "lesson-audio");
  await bindUpload(videoInput, "lesson-video");

  async function saveLesson(){
    const id = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan({
      id: currentLessonId,
      title: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      level: levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner",
      content: canvas?.innerHTML || "",
      media: mediaList
    });

    currentLessonId = id;
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
    savedTick();
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = saveLesson;
  }

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      currentLessonId = "";
      mediaList = [];
      sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = "";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = async () => {
      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const plans = (await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()).filter(p => p.level === level);

      if(!plans.length){
        alert("No saved lesson plans in this level folder yet.");
        return;
      }

      const list = plans.map((p,i)=>`${i+1}. ${p.title || p.name || "Untitled Lesson"}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);
      const selected = plans[Number(choice)-1];

      if(!selected) return;

      currentLessonId = selected.id;
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", currentLessonId);

      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = async () => {
      await saveLesson();
      window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id=" + encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId), "_blank");
    };
  }

  const levelFromUrl = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl && levelInput){
    levelInput.value = levelFromUrl;
  }

  if(currentLessonId){
    const selected = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);

    if(selected){
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    }
  }
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {

  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");

  function addCard(html){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "true";
    card.innerHTML = html;

    canvas.appendChild(card);
    card.focus();
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.onclick = () => {
      const type = btn.getAttribute("data-block");

      btn.style.transform = "scale(.95)";
      setTimeout(() => btn.style.transform = "", 120);

      if(type === "header"){
        addCard("<h1>New Header</h1>");
      }

      if(type === "subheader"){
        addCard("<h2>New Sub Header</h2>");
      }

      if(type === "outline"){
        addCard("<h2>Lesson Outline</h2><ul><li>Warm-up</li><li>Main lesson</li><li>Practice</li></ul>");
      }

      if(type === "title"){
        addCard("<h1>Lesson Title</h1><p>Description...</p>");
      }

      if(type === "objectives"){
        addCard("<h2>Objectives</h2><p><strong>A la fin du cours, l’apprenant doit:</strong></p><ul><li>...</li></ul>");
      }

      if(type === "text"){
        addCard("<p>Write lesson content here...</p>");
      }

      if(type === "image"){
        document.getElementById("imageInput").click();
      }

      if(type === "audio"){
        document.getElementById("audioInput").click();
      }

      if(type === "video"){
        document.getElementById("videoInput").click();
      }
    };
  });

});
</script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_MEDIA_AND_SETTINGS_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function addCard(html){
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "true";
    card.innerHTML = html;

    canvas.appendChild(card);
    card.focus();
  }

  function fileToDataUrl(file, callback){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => callback(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      fileToDataUrl(file, (src) => {
        addCard(`<div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video>`);
      });

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  const newBtn = document.getElementById("newBtn");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn = document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn = document.getElementById("viewBtn");

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      lessonTitle.value = "";
      canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
      const level = lessonLevel.value || "Absolute Beginner";

      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

      const record = {
        id: "LP-" + Date.now(),
        title,
        name: title,
        level,
        content: canvas.innerHTML,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
      };

      saved.push(record);
      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(saved));

      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = () => {
      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");
      const level = lessonLevel.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const files = saved.filter(item => item.level === level);

      if(!files.length){
        const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
        return;
      }

      const list = files.map((item, index) => `${index + 1}. ${item.title || item.name}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);

      const selected = files[Number(choice) - 1];
      if(!selected) return;

      lessonTitle.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle.value.trim() || "Lesson Plan";
      const content = canvas.innerHTML
        .replaceAll('contenteditable="true"', '')
        .replaceAll('class="lesson-card active"', '')
        .replaceAll('class="lesson-card"', '');

      const w = window.open("", "_blank");
      w.document.write(`
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head>
          <meta charset="UTF-8">
          <title>${title}</title>
          <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Sorts+Mill+Goudy&family=Inter:wght@300;400;600;800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
          <style>
            body{
              margin:0;
              background:linear-gradient(180deg,#111827,#05060b);
              color:#f8fafc;
              font-family:Inter,system-ui,sans-serif;
            }
            main{
              max-width:900px;
              margin:0 auto;
              padding:70px 42px;
              line-height:1.75;
            }
            h1,h2,h3{
              font-family:"Sorts Mill Goudy",Georgia,serif;
              font-weight:400;
            }
            img,video{
              max-width:100%;
              border-radius:18px;
              display:block;
              margin:18px 0;
            }
            audio{
              width:100%;
              margin:18px 0;
            }
          /* RESIZABLE LESSON MEDIA */
.lesson-media-wrap{
  display:inline-block;
  max-width:100%;
  resize:both;
  overflow:auto;
  min-width:160px;
  min-height:100px;
  padding:8px;
  border-radius:18px;
  border:1px dashed rgba(232,216,166,.35);
}

.lesson-media-wrap img,
.lesson-media-wrap video{
  width:100%;
  height:auto;
  display:block;
  border-radius:14px;
}

  position:fixed;
