        <script id="LESSON_BUILDER_RESIZE_SAVE_FIX">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const lessonTitle = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const lessonLevel = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function fileToDataUrl(file, cb){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => cb(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <img src="'+src+'" alt="Lesson image">
</div></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><div class="lesson-media-resizer">
  <video src="'+src+'" controls></video>
</div></video></div>`;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${src}" controls></audio>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      fileToDataUrl(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  function showSaveToast(level){
    const toast = document.getElementById("saveToast");
    if(!toast) return;
    toast.textContent = "Saved to " + level + " folder";
    toast.classList.add("show");
    setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove("show"), 2200);
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = () => {
      const title = lessonTitle?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan";
      const level = lessonLevel?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const content = canvas?.innerHTML || "";

      const all = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactLessonPlans") || "[]");

      const existingId = saveBtn.dataset.currentId || "";
      const id = existingId || ("LP-" + Date.now());

      const record = {
        id,
        title,
        name:title,
        level,
        content,
        updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
      };

      const index = all.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
      if(index >= 0) all[index] = record;
      else all.push(record);

      localStorage.setItem("impactLessonPlans", JSON.stringify(all));
      saveBtn.dataset.currentId = id;

      const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
if(tick){
  tick.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
}
    };
  }
});
</script>
<script id="FINAL_IMAGE_UNDO_REPAIR">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const undoBtn = document.getElementById("undoBtn");

  let undoStack = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function saveUndo(){
    undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);
    if(undoStack.length > 50) undoStack.shift();
  }

  function readFile(file, callback){
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => callback(reader.result);
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  }

  function addMediaCard(type, src){
    saveUndo();
    removeEmpty();

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";

    if(type === "image"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <img src="${src}" alt="Lesson image">
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "video"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <div class="lesson-media-resizer">
          <video src="${src}" controls></video>
        </div>
      `;
    }

    if(type === "audio"){
      card.innerHTML = `
        <audio src="${src}" controls></audio>
      `;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  if(imageInput){
    imageInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("image", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(videoInput){
    videoInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("video", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  if(audioInput){
    audioInput.onchange = (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;
      readFile(file, src => addMediaCard("audio", src));
      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const type = btn.dataset.block;
      if(!["image","audio","video"].includes(type)){
        saveUndo();
      }
    }, true);
  });

  if(undoBtn){
    undoBtn.textContent = "↶";
    undoBtn.title = "Undo";
    undoBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!undoStack.length) return;
      canvas.innerHTML = undoStack.pop();
    };
  }
});
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-storage-final-001"></script>

<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>

<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>
<script id="LESSON_BUILDER_FIREBASE_FINAL">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");
  const titleInput = document.getElementById("lessonTitle");
  const levelInput = document.getElementById("lessonLevel");
  const saveBtn = document.getElementById("saveBtn");
  const editBtn = document.getElementById("editBtn");
  const viewBtn = document.getElementById("viewBtn");
  const newBtn = document.getElementById("newBtn");

  const imageInput = document.getElementById("imageInput");
  const audioInput = document.getElementById("audioInput");
  const videoInput = document.getElementById("videoInput");

  let currentLessonId =
    new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit") ||
    sessionStorage.getItem("impactEditingLessonId") ||
    "";

  let mediaList = [];

  function removeEmpty(){
    const empty = canvas?.querySelector(".empty-state");
    if(empty) empty.remove();
  }

  function savedTick(){
    const tick = document.getElementById("saveTick");
    if(tick){
      tick.classList.add("show");
      setTimeout(() => tick.classList.remove("show"), 1400);
    }
  }

  function addMediaCard(media){
    removeEmpty();
    mediaList.push(media);

    const card = document.createElement("article");
    card.className = "lesson-card lesson-media-card";
    card.contentEditable = "false";
    card.dataset.storagePath = media.path || "";
    card.dataset.mediaUrl = media.url || "";

    if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("image")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><img src="${media.url}" alt="${media.name || "Lesson image"}"></div>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("audio")){
      card.innerHTML = `<audio src="${media.url}" controls></audio>`;
    } else if((media.mimeType || "").startsWith("video")){
      card.innerHTML = `<div class="lesson-media-resizer"><video src="${media.url}" controls></video></div>`;
    } else {
      card.innerHTML = `<a href="${media.url}" target="_blank">${media.name || "Uploaded file"}</a>`;
    }

    canvas.appendChild(card);
  }

  async function bindUpload(input, folder){
    if(!input) return;

    input.onchange = async (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if(!file) return;

      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const lessonTitle = titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson";
      const subfolder = level + "/" + lessonTitle;

      const media = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.uploadFile(file, folder, subfolder);
      addMediaCard(media);

      e.target.value = "";
    };
  }

  await bindUpload(imageInput, "lesson-images");
  await bindUpload(audioInput, "lesson-audio");
  await bindUpload(videoInput, "lesson-video");

  async function saveLesson(){
    const id = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.saveLessonPlan({
      id: currentLessonId,
      title: titleInput?.value.trim() || "Untitled Lesson Plan",
      level: levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner",
      content: canvas?.innerHTML || "",
      media: mediaList
    });

    currentLessonId = id;
    sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", id);
    savedTick();
  }

  if(saveBtn){
    saveBtn.onclick = saveLesson;
  }

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      currentLessonId = "";
      mediaList = [];
      sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = "";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = async () => {
      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const plans = (await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()).filter(p => p.level === level);

      if(!plans.length){
        alert("No saved lesson plans in this level folder yet.");
        return;
      }

      const list = plans.map((p,i)=>`${i+1}. ${p.title || p.name || "Untitled Lesson"}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);
      const selected = plans[Number(choice)-1];

      if(!selected) return;

      currentLessonId = selected.id;
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", currentLessonId);

      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = async () => {
      await saveLesson();
      window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id=" + encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId), "_blank");
    };
  }

  const levelFromUrl = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl && levelInput){
    levelInput.value = levelFromUrl;
  }

  if(currentLessonId){
    const selected = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);

    if(selected){
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    }
  }
});
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-task-menu-patch.js"></script><script id="lesson-template-builder-loader">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
  try{
    const plan=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan")||"{}");
    if(!plan || plan.type!=="template") return;

    const titleInput=document.getElementById("lessonTitle") || document.querySelector("input[placeholder*='title' i]");
    const levelInput=document.getElementById("lessonLevel") || document.querySelector("select");
    const canvas=document.getElementById("canvas") || document.querySelector(".canvas,.lesson-canvas");

    if(titleInput) titleInput.value=plan.title || "";
    if(levelInput) levelInput.value=plan.level || "Absolute Beginner";

    if(canvas && !canvas.dataset.templateLoaded){
      canvas.dataset.templateLoaded="yes";
      canvas.innerHTML=`
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <h2>${plan.title || "Lesson Template"}</h2>
          <p><strong>Objective:</strong> ${plan.objective || ""}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <p><strong>Lesson Flow:</strong> ${plan.flow || ""}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <p><strong>Materials:</strong> ${plan.materials || ""}</p>
        </article>
      `;
    }
  }catch(e){
    console.warn("Template loader skipped",e);
  }
});
</script>

</body>
        </html>
      `);
      w.document.close();
    };
  }
});
</script>

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
  const canvas = document.getElementById("canvas");

  await bindUpload(imageInput, "lesson-images");

  async function saveLesson(){

  }

  if(newBtn){
    newBtn.onclick = () => {
      if(!confirm("Start a new lesson plan?")) return;
      currentLessonId = "";
      mediaList = [];
      sessionStorage.removeItem("impactEditingLessonId");
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = "";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add lesson blocks from the left. Each block will appear here as an editable card.</div>`;
    };
  }

  if(editBtn){
    editBtn.onclick = async () => {
      const level = levelInput?.value || "Absolute Beginner";
      const plans = (await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()).filter(p => p.level === level);

      if(!plans.length){
        alert("No saved lesson plans in this level folder yet.");
        return;
      }

      const list = plans.map((p,i)=>`${i+1}. ${p.title || p.name || "Untitled Lesson"}`).join("\n");
      const choice = prompt("Select lesson plan number:\n\n" + list);
      const selected = plans[Number(choice)-1];

      if(!selected) return;

      currentLessonId = selected.id;
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId", currentLessonId);

      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    };
  }

  if(viewBtn){
    viewBtn.onclick = async () => {
      await saveLesson();
      window.open("/teacher/lesson-view.html?id=" + encodeURIComponent(currentLessonId), "_blank");
    };
  }

  const levelFromUrl = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("level");
  if(levelFromUrl && levelInput){
    levelInput.value = levelFromUrl;
  }

  if(currentLessonId){
    const selected = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(currentLessonId);

    if(selected){
      mediaList = selected.media || [];
      if(titleInput) titleInput.value = selected.title || selected.name || "";
      if(levelInput) levelInput.value = selected.level || "Absolute Beginner";
      if(canvas) canvas.innerHTML = selected.content || "";
    }
  }
});
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-task-menu-patch.js"></script><script id="lesson-template-builder-loader">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
  try{
    const plan=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan")||"{}");
    if(!plan || plan.type!=="template") return;

    const titleInput=document.getElementById("lessonTitle") || document.querySelector("input[placeholder*='title' i]");
    const levelInput=document.getElementById("lessonLevel") || document.querySelector("select");
    const canvas=document.getElementById("canvas") || document.querySelector(".canvas,.lesson-canvas");

    if(titleInput) titleInput.value=plan.title || "";
    if(levelInput) levelInput.value=plan.level || "Absolute Beginner";

    if(canvas && !canvas.dataset.templateLoaded){
      canvas.dataset.templateLoaded="yes";
      canvas.innerHTML=`
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <h2>${plan.title || "Lesson Template"}</h2>
          <p><strong>Objective:</strong> ${plan.objective || ""}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <p><strong>Lesson Flow:</strong> ${plan.flow || ""}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="lesson-card" contenteditable="true">
          <p><strong>Materials:</strong> ${plan.materials || ""}</p>
        </article>
      `;
    }
  }catch(e){
    console.warn("Template loader skipped",e);
  }
});
</script>

<script>
let currentDoc = "";

function addText(){
  const el = document.createElement("p");
  el.innerText = "Text...";
  document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(el);
  autosave();
}

function addHeader(){
  const el = document.createElement("h1");
  el.innerText = "Header";
  document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(el);
  autosave();
}

function addSub(){
  const el = document.createElement("h3");
  el.innerText = "Sub Header";
  document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(el);
  autosave();
}

function addImage(){
  const input = document.createElement("input");
  input.type = "file";
  input.accept="image/*";
  input.onchange = e=>{
    const img = document.createElement("img");
    img.src = URL.createObjectURL(e.target.files[0]);
    img.style.maxWidth="100%";
    document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(img);
    autosave();
  }
  input.click();
}

function addVideo(){
  const url = prompt("Paste video URL");
  if(!url)return;
  const vid = document.createElement("video");
  vid.src = url;
  vid.controls = true;
  vid.style.maxWidth="100%";
  document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(vid);
  autosave();
}

function addAudio(){
  const url = prompt("Paste audio URL");
  if(!url)return;
  const aud = document.createElement("audio");
  aud.src = url;
  aud.controls = true;
  document.getElementById("slide").appendChild(aud);
  autosave();
}

function saveDoc(){
  const name = prompt("Name this lesson");
  if(!name)return;
  currentDoc = name;
  localStorage.setItem("lesson_"+name, document.getElementById("slide").innerHTML);
}

function autosave(){
  if(currentDoc){
    localStorage.setItem("lesson_"+currentDoc, document.getElementById("slide").innerHTML);
  }
}

function newDoc(){
  document.getElementById("slide").innerHTML="";
  currentDoc="";
}

function editDoc(){
  const name = prompt("Enter lesson name");
  const data = localStorage.getItem("lesson_"+name);
  if(data){
    currentDoc = name;
    document.getElementById("slide").innerHTML = data;
  }
}

function viewDoc(){
  alert("View mode coming next");
}
</script>

<div class="impact-confirm-backdrop" id="impactConfirmModal">
  <div class="impact-confirm-card">
    <h3>Delete template?</h3>
    <p id="impactConfirmMessage">This will remove the template from this folder.</p>
    <div class="impact-confirm-actions">
      <button type="button" id="impactConfirmCancel">Cancel</button>
      <button type="button" class="danger" id="impactConfirmOk">Delete</button>
    </div>

<script src="/js/impact-global-bg.js"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-page-nav.js"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-firebase-store.js?v=firebase-final-001"></script>

<script>
(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  const templateBase=[
    {key:"speaking-starter",title:"Template 1 — Speaking Starter",objective:"Learners practise simple oral production from the first minutes of class.",flow:"Warm-up → teacher model → repetition → guided speaking → independent speaking → quick correction.",materials:"Speaking prompts, name cards, simple question frames."},
    {key:"vocabulary-builder",title:"Template 2 — Vocabulary Builder",objective:"Learners use new vocabulary confidently in short spoken sentences.",flow:"Picture prompt → vocabulary drilling → sentence building → oral practice → mini performance check.",materials:"Picture cards, vocabulary list, sentence frames."},
    {key:"assessment-prep",title:"Template 3 — Assessment Prep",objective:"Learners review weak areas and practise assessment-style tasks.",flow:"Quick diagnostic → correction → guided practice → individual attempt → feedback.",materials:"Review worksheet, assessment prompts, correction notes."}
  ];

  function impactConfirm(message){
    return new Promise(resolve=>{
      const modal=document.getElementById("impactConfirmModal");
      const msg=document.getElementById("impactConfirmMessage");
      const ok=document.getElementById("impactConfirmOk");
      const cancel=document.getElementById("impactConfirmCancel");

      msg.textContent=message;
      modal.classList.add("show");

      const close=(result)=>{
        modal.classList.remove("show");
        ok.onclick=null;
        cancel.onclick=null;
        modal.onclick=null;
        resolve(result);
      };

      ok.onclick=()=>close(true);
      cancel.onclick=()=>close(false);
      modal.onclick=(e)=>{ if(e.target===modal) close(false); };
    });
  }

  function deletedTemplates(){
    try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates")||"[]")}
    catch(e){return []}
  }

  function saveDeletedTemplate(id){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    deleted.push(id);
    localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates",JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));
  }

  function templatePlansFor(level){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    return templateBase.map(t=>({
      id:`template-${level.replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/\./g,"-").toLowerCase()}-${t.key}`,
      level,
      title:t.title,
      type:"template",
      isTemplate:true,
      objective:t.objective,
      flow:t.flow,
      materials:t.materials
    })).filter(t=>!deleted.includes(t.id));
  }

  async function safeGetPlans(){
    try{return await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()}
    catch(e){console.warn(e);return []}
  }

  async function render(){
    const savedPlans=await safeGetPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=[...templatePlansFor(level),...savedPlans.filter(p=>p.level===level)];
      const fileHtml=files.map(file=>`
        <div class="lesson-file-row">
          <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
          <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-view-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">🔎</button>
          <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-edit-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">✍🏽</button>
          <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">❌</button>
        </div>`).join("");

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  grid.addEventListener("click",async e=>{
    const deleteBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-delete-btn");
    const viewBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-view-btn,.file-pill");
    const editBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-edit-btn");
    const card=e.target.closest(".level-card");

    if(deleteBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      const id=deleteBtn.dataset.id;
      const isTemplate=deleteBtn.dataset.template==="yes";

      if(isTemplate){
        const ok=await impactConfirm("Delete this template from the folder?");
        if(!ok) return;
        saveDeletedTemplate(id);
        await render();
        return;
      }

      const ok=await impactConfirm("Delete this lesson plan?");
      if(!ok) return;
      await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);
      await render();
      return;
    }

    if(viewBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      const row=viewBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
      const id=viewBtn.dataset.id;
      const level=viewBtn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
      const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
      const selected=template || {id,title:row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim(),level,type:"saved"};
      localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);
      location.href="/teacher/lesson-plan-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      return;
    }

    if(editBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      const row=editBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
      const id=editBtn.dataset.id;
      const level=editBtn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
      const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
      const selected=template || {id,title:row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim(),level,type:"saved"};
      localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);
      location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      return;
    }

    if(card){
      document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open")});
      card.classList.toggle("open");
      grid.classList.toggle("folder-focus-active",!!document.querySelector(".level-card.open"));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener("click",e=>{
    if(e.target.closest(".level-card") || e.target.closest(".create-btn") || e.target.closest(".impact-confirm-card")) return;
    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card.open").forEach(card=>card.classList.remove("open"));
    grid.classList.remove("folder-focus-active");
  });

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  await render();
})();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-round-icons.js?v=001"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
<script id="lesson-plan-delete-fix">
document.addEventListener("click", async function(e){

  const btn = e.target.closest(".delete-btn,.delete-plan,[data-delete],[data-delete-id]");

  if(!btn) return;

  const txt = (btn.textContent || "").toLowerCase();

  if(
    !txt.includes("delete") &&
    !btn.classList.contains("delete-btn") &&
    !btn.classList.contains("delete-plan")
  ){
    return;
  }

  e.preventDefault();
  e.stopPropagation();

  const id =
    btn.dataset.delete ||
    btn.dataset.deleteId ||
    btn.dataset.id ||
    btn.closest("[data-id]")?.dataset?.id;

  if(!id){
    alert("Could not find lesson plan ID.");
    return;
  }

  if(!confirm("Delete this lesson plan?")) return;

  try{

    if(window.firebase && firebase.firestore){

      await firebase.firestore()
        .collection("lessonPlans")
        .doc(id)
        .delete();
    }

    const row =
      btn.closest(".lesson-row,.lesson-item,.template-row,.card");

    if(row) row.remove();

  }catch(err){

    console.error(err);
    alert("Delete failed.");
  }

}, true);
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  async function render(){
    const plans=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=plans.filter(p=>p.level===level);
      const fileHtml=files.length
        ? files.map(file=>`
          <div class="lesson-file-row">
            <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
            <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-delete-id="${file.id}" type="button">Delete</button>
          </div>`).join("")
        : `<div class="empty-note">No lesson plans saved yet.</div>`;

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(card=>{
      card.onclick=e=>{
        if(e.target.closest("button")) return;
        document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open")});
        card.classList.toggle("open");
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".file-pill").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",btn.dataset.id);
        location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(btn.dataset.id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-delete-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=async e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        if(!confirm("Delete this lesson plan?")) return;
        await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(btn.dataset.deleteId);
        await render();
      };
    });
  }

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  await render();
})();
</script>

<script>
function impactConfirm(message){
  return new Promise(resolve=>{
    const modal=document.getElementById("impactConfirmModal");
    const msg=document.getElementById("impactConfirmMessage");
    const ok=document.getElementById("impactConfirmOk");
    const cancel=document.getElementById("impactConfirmCancel");

    msg.textContent=message || "Are you sure?";
    modal.classList.add("show");

    function close(result){
      modal.classList.remove("show");
      ok.onclick=null;
      cancel.onclick=null;
      modal.onclick=null;
      resolve(result);
    }

    ok.onclick=()=>close(true);
    cancel.onclick=()=>close(false);
    modal.onclick=e=>{
      if(e.target===modal) close(false);
    };
  });
}

(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  const templateBase=[
    {
      key:"speaking-starter",
      title:"Template 1 — Speaking Starter",
      objective:"Learners practise simple oral production from the first minutes of class.",
      flow:"Warm-up → teacher model → repetition → guided speaking → independent speaking → quick correction.",
      materials:"Speaking prompts, name cards, simple question frames."
    },
    {
      key:"vocabulary-builder",
      title:"Template 2 — Vocabulary Builder",
      objective:"Learners use new vocabulary confidently in short spoken sentences.",
      flow:"Picture prompt → vocabulary drilling → sentence building → oral practice → mini performance check.",
      materials:"Picture cards, vocabulary list, sentence frames."
    },
    {
      key:"assessment-prep",
      title:"Template 3 — Assessment Prep",
      objective:"Learners review weak areas and practise assessment-style tasks.",
      flow:"Quick diagnostic → correction → guided practice → individual attempt → feedback.",
      materials:"Review worksheet, assessment prompts, correction notes."
    }
  ];

  function deletedTemplates(){
    try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates")||"[]")}
    catch(e){return []}
  }

  function templatePlansFor(level){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    return templateBase
      .map(t=>({
        id:`template-${level.replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/\./g,"-").toLowerCase()}-${t.key}`,
        level,
        title:t.title,
        type:"template",
        isTemplate:true,
        objective:t.objective,
        flow:t.flow,
        materials:t.materials
      }))
      .filter(t=>!deleted.includes(t.id));
  }

  async function safeGetPlans(){
    try{
      return await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans();
    }catch(e){
      console.warn("Could not load lesson plans:",e);
      return [];
    }
  }

  async function render(){
    const savedPlans=await safeGetPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=[...templatePlansFor(level), ...savedPlans.filter(p=>p.level===level)];
      const fileHtml=files.length
        ? files.map(file=>`
          <div class="lesson-file-row">
            <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
            <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-view-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">🔎</button>
            <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-edit-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">✍🏽</button>
            <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-delete-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">❌</button>
          </div>`).join("")
        : `<div class="empty-note">No lesson plans saved yet.</div>`;

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(card=>{
      card.onclick=e=>{
        if(e.target.closest("button")) return;

        document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{
          if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open");
        });

        card.classList.toggle("open");

        const anyOpen=!!document.querySelector(".level-card.open");
        grid.classList.toggle("folder-focus-active",anyOpen);

        sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".file-pill,.lesson-view-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        const row=btn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
        const title=row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim();
        const id=btn.dataset.id;
        const level=btn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        const selected={
          id,
          title,
          level,
          type:isTemplate ? "template" : "saved"
        };

        const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
        if(template) Object.assign(selected,template);

        localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);

        location.href="/teacher/lesson-plan-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-edit-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        const row=btn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
        const title=row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim();
        const id=btn.dataset.id;
        const level=btn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        const selected={
          id,
          title,
          level,
          type:isTemplate ? "template" : "saved"
        };

        const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
        if(template) Object.assign(selected,template);

        localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);

        location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-delete-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=async e=>{
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        const id=btn.dataset.deleteId;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        if(isTemplate){
          if(!(await impactConfirm("Delete this template from the folder?"))) return;
          const deleted=deletedTemplates();
          deleted.push(id);
          localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates",JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));
          await render();
          return;
        }

        if(!(await impactConfirm("Delete this lesson plan?"))) return;
        await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);
        await render();
      };
    });
  }

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  document.addEventListener("click",function(e){
    if(e.target.closest(".level-card") || e.target.closest(".create-btn")) return;

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card.open").forEach(card=>card.classList.remove("open"));
    grid.classList.remove("folder-focus-active");
  });

  await render();
})();
</script>




<script id="lesson-delete-final-fix">
document.addEventListener("click", async function(e){
  const deleteBtn = e.target.closest(".lesson-delete-btn");
  if(!deleteBtn) return;

  e.preventDefault();
  e.stopPropagation();
  e.stopImmediatePropagation();

  const id = deleteBtn.dataset.deleteId;
  const isTemplate = deleteBtn.dataset.template === "yes";
  const row = deleteBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
  const card = deleteBtn.closest(".level-card");

  async function askDelete(message){
    if(typeof impactConfirm === "function"){
      return await impactConfirm(message);
    }
    return window.confirm(message);
  }

  if(isTemplate){
    const ok = await askDelete("Delete this template from the folder?");
    if(!ok) return;

    const deleted = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates") || "[]");
    deleted.push(id);
    localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates", JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));

    if(row) row.remove();

    if(card){
      const remaining = card.querySelectorAll(".lesson-file-row").length;
      const count = card.querySelector("p");
      if(count){
        count.textContent = remaining + " lesson plan" + (remaining === 1 ? "" : "s");
      }
    }

    return;
  }

  const ok = await askDelete("Delete this lesson plan?");
  if(!ok) return;

  try{
    await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);

    if(row) row.remove();

    if(card){
      const remaining = card.querySelectorAll(".lesson-file-row").length;
      const count = card.querySelector("p");
      if(count){
        count.textContent = remaining + " lesson plan" + (remaining === 1 ? "" : "s");
      }
    }
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    alert("Could not delete this lesson plan.");
  }
}, true);
</script>

</body>
</html>

<style>

<script>
(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  async function render(){
    const plans=await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=plans.filter(p=>p.level===level);
      const fileHtml=files.length
        ? files.map(file=>`
          <div class="lesson-file-row">
            <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
            <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-delete-id="${file.id}" type="button">Delete</button>
          </div>`).join("")
        : `<div class="empty-note">No lesson plans saved yet.</div>`;

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(card=>{
      card.onclick=e=>{
        if(e.target.closest("button")) return;
        document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open")});
        card.classList.toggle("open");
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".file-pill").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",btn.dataset.id);
        location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(btn.dataset.id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-delete-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=async e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        if(!confirm("Delete this lesson plan?")) return;
        await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(btn.dataset.deleteId);
        await render();
      };
    });
  }

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  await render();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

    <p id="impactConfirmMessage">This will remove the template from this folder.</p>
    <div class="impact-confirm-actions">

      <button type="button" class="danger" id="impactConfirmOk">Delete</button>

<script>
function impactConfirm(message){
  return new Promise(resolve=>{
    const modal=document.getElementById("impactConfirmModal");
    const msg=document.getElementById("impactConfirmMessage");
    const ok=document.getElementById("impactConfirmOk");
    const cancel=document.getElementById("impactConfirmCancel");

    msg.textContent=message || "Are you sure?";
    modal.classList.add("show");

    function close(result){
      modal.classList.remove("show");
      ok.onclick=null;
      cancel.onclick=null;
      modal.onclick=null;
      resolve(result);
    }

    ok.onclick=()=>close(true);
    cancel.onclick=()=>close(false);
    modal.onclick=e=>{
      if(e.target===modal) close(false);
    };
  });
}

(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  const templateBase=[
    {
      key:"speaking-starter",
      title:"Template 1 — Speaking Starter",
      objective:"Learners practise simple oral production from the first minutes of class.",
      flow:"Warm-up → teacher model → repetition → guided speaking → independent speaking → quick correction.",
      materials:"Speaking prompts, name cards, simple question frames."
    },
    {
      key:"vocabulary-builder",
      title:"Template 2 — Vocabulary Builder",
      objective:"Learners use new vocabulary confidently in short spoken sentences.",
      flow:"Picture prompt → vocabulary drilling → sentence building → oral practice → mini performance check.",
      materials:"Picture cards, vocabulary list, sentence frames."
    },
    {
      key:"assessment-prep",
      title:"Template 3 — Assessment Prep",
      objective:"Learners review weak areas and practise assessment-style tasks.",
      flow:"Quick diagnostic → correction → guided practice → individual attempt → feedback.",
      materials:"Review worksheet, assessment prompts, correction notes."
    }
  ];

  function deletedTemplates(){
    try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates")||"[]")}
    catch(e){return []}
  }

  function templatePlansFor(level){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    return templateBase
      .map(t=>({
        id:`template-${level.replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/\./g,"-").toLowerCase()}-${t.key}`,
        level,
        title:t.title,
        type:"template",
        isTemplate:true,
        objective:t.objective,
        flow:t.flow,
        materials:t.materials
      }))
      .filter(t=>!deleted.includes(t.id));
  }

  async function safeGetPlans(){
    try{
      return await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans();
    }catch(e){
      console.warn("Could not load lesson plans:",e);
      return [];
    }
  }

  async function render(){
    const savedPlans=await safeGetPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=[...templatePlansFor(level), ...savedPlans.filter(p=>p.level===level)];
      const fileHtml=files.length
        ? files.map(file=>`
          <div class="lesson-file-row">
            <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
            <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-view-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">🔎</button>
            <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-edit-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">✍🏽</button>
            <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-delete-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">❌</button>
          </div>`).join("")
        : `<div class="empty-note">No lesson plans saved yet.</div>`;

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(card=>{
      card.onclick=e=>{
        if(e.target.closest("button")) return;

        document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{
          if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open");
        });

        card.classList.toggle("open");

        const anyOpen=!!document.querySelector(".level-card.open");
        grid.classList.toggle("folder-focus-active",anyOpen);

        sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".file-pill,.lesson-view-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        const row=btn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
        const title=row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim();
        const id=btn.dataset.id;
        const level=btn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        const selected={
          id,
          title,
          level,
          type:isTemplate ? "template" : "saved"
        };

        const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
        if(template) Object.assign(selected,template);

        localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);

        location.href="/teacher/lesson-plan-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-edit-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=e=>{
        e.stopPropagation();
        const row=btn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
        const title=row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim();
        const id=btn.dataset.id;
        const level=btn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        const selected={
          id,
          title,
          level,
          type:isTemplate ? "template" : "saved"
        };

        const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
        if(template) Object.assign(selected,template);

        localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
        sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);

        location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      };
    });

    document.querySelectorAll(".lesson-delete-btn").forEach(btn=>{
      btn.onclick=async e=>{
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        const id=btn.dataset.deleteId;
        const isTemplate=btn.dataset.template==="yes";

        if(isTemplate){
          if(!(await impactConfirm("Delete this template from the folder?"))) return;
          const deleted=deletedTemplates();
          deleted.push(id);
          localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates",JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));
          await render();
          return;
        }

        if(!(await impactConfirm("Delete this lesson plan?"))) return;
        await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);
        await render();
      };
    });
  }

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  document.addEventListener("click",function(e){
    if(e.target.closest(".level-card") || e.target.closest(".create-btn")) return;

    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card.open").forEach(card=>card.classList.remove("open"));
    grid.classList.remove("folder-focus-active");
  });

  await render();
})();
</script>

<script id="lesson-delete-final-fix">
document.addEventListener("click", async function(e){
  const deleteBtn = e.target.closest(".lesson-delete-btn");
  if(!deleteBtn) return;

  e.preventDefault();
  e.stopPropagation();
  e.stopImmediatePropagation();

  const id = deleteBtn.dataset.deleteId;
  const isTemplate = deleteBtn.dataset.template === "yes";
  const row = deleteBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
  const card = deleteBtn.closest(".level-card");

  async function askDelete(message){
    if(typeof impactConfirm === "function"){
      return await impactConfirm(message);
    }
    return window.confirm(message);
  }

  if(isTemplate){
    const ok = await askDelete("Delete this template from the folder?");
    if(!ok) return;

    const deleted = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates") || "[]");
    deleted.push(id);
    localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates", JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));

    if(row) row.remove();

    if(card){
      const remaining = card.querySelectorAll(".lesson-file-row").length;
      const count = card.querySelector("p");
      if(count){
        count.textContent = remaining + " lesson plan" + (remaining === 1 ? "" : "s");
      }
    }

    return;
  }

  const ok = await askDelete("Delete this lesson plan?");
  if(!ok) return;

  try{
    await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);

    if(row) row.remove();

    if(card){
      const remaining = card.querySelectorAll(".lesson-file-row").length;
      const count = card.querySelector("p");
      if(count){
        count.textContent = remaining + " lesson plan" + (remaining === 1 ? "" : "s");
      }
    }
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    alert("Could not delete this lesson plan.");
  }
}, true);
</script>

</body>
</html>

    <h3>Delete template?</h3>
    <p id="impactConfirmMessage">This will remove the template from this folder.</p>
    <div class="impact-confirm-actions">

      <button type="button" class="danger" id="impactConfirmOk">Delete</button>

<script>
(async function(){
  const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
  const grid=document.getElementById("levelGrid");
  const createBtn=document.getElementById("createBtn");

  const templateBase=[
    {key:"speaking-starter",title:"Template 1 — Speaking Starter",objective:"Learners practise simple oral production from the first minutes of class.",flow:"Warm-up → teacher model → repetition → guided speaking → independent speaking → quick correction.",materials:"Speaking prompts, name cards, simple question frames."},
    {key:"vocabulary-builder",title:"Template 2 — Vocabulary Builder",objective:"Learners use new vocabulary confidently in short spoken sentences.",flow:"Picture prompt → vocabulary drilling → sentence building → oral practice → mini performance check.",materials:"Picture cards, vocabulary list, sentence frames."},
    {key:"assessment-prep",title:"Template 3 — Assessment Prep",objective:"Learners review weak areas and practise assessment-style tasks.",flow:"Quick diagnostic → correction → guided practice → individual attempt → feedback.",materials:"Review worksheet, assessment prompts, correction notes."}
  ];

  function impactConfirm(message){
    return new Promise(resolve=>{
      const modal=document.getElementById("impactConfirmModal");
      const msg=document.getElementById("impactConfirmMessage");
      const ok=document.getElementById("impactConfirmOk");
      const cancel=document.getElementById("impactConfirmCancel");

      msg.textContent=message;
      modal.classList.add("show");

      const close=(result)=>{
        modal.classList.remove("show");
        ok.onclick=null;
        cancel.onclick=null;
        modal.onclick=null;
        resolve(result);
      };

      ok.onclick=()=>close(true);
      cancel.onclick=()=>close(false);
      modal.onclick=(e)=>{ if(e.target===modal) close(false); };
    });
  }

  function deletedTemplates(){
    try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates")||"[]")}
    catch(e){return []}
  }

  function saveDeletedTemplate(id){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    deleted.push(id);
    localStorage.setItem("impactDeletedLessonTemplates",JSON.stringify([...new Set(deleted)]));
  }

  function templatePlansFor(level){
    const deleted=deletedTemplates();
    return templateBase.map(t=>({
      id:`template-${level.replace(/\s+/g,"-").replace(/\./g,"-").toLowerCase()}-${t.key}`,
      level,
      title:t.title,
      type:"template",
      isTemplate:true,
      objective:t.objective,
      flow:t.flow,
      materials:t.materials
    })).filter(t=>!deleted.includes(t.id));
  }

  async function safeGetPlans(){
    try{return await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlans()}
    catch(e){console.warn(e);return []}
  }

  async function render(){
    const savedPlans=await safeGetPlans();

    grid.innerHTML=levels.map(level=>{
      const files=[...templatePlansFor(level),...savedPlans.filter(p=>p.level===level)];
      const fileHtml=files.map(file=>`
        <div class="lesson-file-row">
          <button class="file-pill" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">${file.title || file.name || "Untitled Lesson"}</button>
          <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-view-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">🔎</button>
          <button class="lesson-action-btn lesson-edit-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">✍🏽</button>
          <button class="lesson-delete-btn" data-id="${file.id}" data-template="${file.isTemplate ? "yes" : "no"}" type="button">❌</button>
        </div>`).join("");

      return `<article class="level-card" data-level="${level}">
        <h2>${level}</h2>
        <p>${files.length} lesson plan${files.length===1?"":"s"}</p>
        <div class="file-list">${fileHtml}</div>
      </article>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  grid.addEventListener("click",async e=>{
    const deleteBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-delete-btn");
    const viewBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-view-btn,.file-pill");
    const editBtn=e.target.closest(".lesson-edit-btn");
    const card=e.target.closest(".level-card");

    if(deleteBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();

      const id=deleteBtn.dataset.id;
      const isTemplate=deleteBtn.dataset.template==="yes";

      if(isTemplate){
        const ok=await impactConfirm("Delete this template from the folder?");
        if(!ok) return;
        saveDeletedTemplate(id);
        await render();
        return;
      }

      const ok=await impactConfirm("Delete this lesson plan?");
      if(!ok) return;
      await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.deleteLessonPlan(id);
      await render();
      return;
    }

    if(viewBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      const row=viewBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
      const id=viewBtn.dataset.id;
      const level=viewBtn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
      const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
      const selected=template || {id,title:row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim(),level,type:"saved"};
      localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);
      location.href="/teacher/lesson-plan-view.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      return;
    }

    if(editBtn){
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      const row=editBtn.closest(".lesson-file-row");
      const id=editBtn.dataset.id;
      const level=editBtn.closest(".level-card").dataset.level;
      const template=templatePlansFor(level).find(t=>t.id===id);
      const selected=template || {id,title:row.querySelector(".file-pill").textContent.trim(),level,type:"saved"};
      localStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonPlan",JSON.stringify(selected));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactEditingLessonId",id);
      location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?edit="+encodeURIComponent(id);
      return;
    }

    if(card){
      document.querySelectorAll(".level-card").forEach(c=>{if(c!==card)c.classList.remove("open")});
      card.classList.toggle("open");
      grid.classList.toggle("folder-focus-active",!!document.querySelector(".level-card.open"));
      sessionStorage.setItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel",card.dataset.level);
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener("click",e=>{
    if(e.target.closest(".level-card") || e.target.closest(".create-btn") || e.target.closest(".impact-confirm-card")) return;
    document.querySelectorAll(".level-card.open").forEach(card=>card.classList.remove("open"));
    grid.classList.remove("folder-focus-active");
  });

  createBtn.onclick=()=>{
    const selected=sessionStorage.getItem("impactSelectedLessonLevel") || "Absolute Beginner";
    location.href="/teacher/lesson-builder.html?level="+encodeURIComponent(selected);
  };

  await render();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
(async function(){
  const id = new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("id");
  const title = document.getElementById("title");
  const content = document.getElementById("content");

  const plan = await window.ImpactFirebaseStore.getLessonPlan(id);

  if(!plan){
    content.innerHTML = "Lesson plan not found.";
    return;
  }

  title.textContent = plan.title || plan.name || "Lesson Plan";
  content.innerHTML = plan.content || "";
})();
</script>

<input id="imageInput" type="file" accept="image/*" style="display:none">
<input id="audioInput" type="file" accept="audio/*" style="display:none">
<input id="videoInput" type="file" accept="video/*" style="display:none">

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-firestore-compat.js"></script>
<script src="/__/firebase/init.js"></script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
const db=firebase.firestore();
const canvas=document.getElementById("canvas");
const titleInput=document.getElementById("testTitle");
const saveTick=document.getElementById("saveTick");
let currentId=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("edit")||"";
let selectedCard=null,allSelected=false,undoStack=[],draggedCard=null;

function tick(){saveTick.classList.add("show");setTimeout(()=>saveTick.classList.remove("show"),1300)}
function clearEmpty(){const e=canvas.querySelector(".empty-state");if(e)e.remove()}
function allCards(){return Array.from(canvas.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card"))}
function targetCards(){return allSelected?allCards():(selectedCard?[selectedCard]:[])}
function selectCard(card){allSelected=false;canvas.classList.remove("all-selected");selectedCard=card;allCards().forEach(c=>c.classList.remove("active"));card.classList.add("active")}
function selectAll(){if(!allCards().length)return;allSelected=true;selectedCard=null;canvas.classList.add("all-selected");allCards().forEach(c=>c.classList.add("active"))}
function pushUndo(){undoStack.push(canvas.innerHTML);if(undoStack.length>30)undoStack.shift()}

function bindCard(card){
card.setAttribute("draggable","true");
card.onclick=e=>{e.stopPropagation();selectCard(card)};
card.oninput=()=>{};
const del=card.querySelector(".delete-card");
if(del){del.onclick=e=>{e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();pushUndo();card.remove();if(!allCards().length)canvas.innerHTML='<div class="empty-state">Add placement test blocks from the left. Click inside the canvas to select all blocks for formatting.</div>'}};

card.ondragstart=e=>{draggedCard=card;card.classList.add("dragging");e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed="move"};
card.ondragend=()=>{card.classList.remove("dragging");allCards().forEach(c=>c.classList.remove("drag-over"));draggedCard=null};
card.ondragover=e=>{e.preventDefault();if(draggedCard&&draggedCard!==card)card.classList.add("drag-over")};
card.ondragleave=()=>card.classList.remove("drag-over");
card.ondrop=e=>{e.preventDefault();card.classList.remove("drag-over");if(!draggedCard||draggedCard===card)return;pushUndo();const r=card.getBoundingClientRect();if(e.clientY>r.top+r.height/2)card.after(draggedCard);else card.before(draggedCard)};
}

function createCard(html,isGap){
const card=document.createElement("article");
card.className="lesson-card"+(isGap?" gap-card":"");
card.contentEditable=isGap?"false":"true";
card.innerHTML='<button class="delete-card" contenteditable="false" type="button">×</button>'+html;
bindCard(card);
return card;
}

function addCard(html,isGap=false){
pushUndo();clearEmpty();
const card=createCard(html,isGap);
if(isGap&&selectedCard&&canvas.contains(selectedCard))selectedCard.after(card);else canvas.appendChild(card);
selectCard(card);
}

function template(type){
if(type==="header")return '<h1>PLACEMENT TEST</h1>';
if(type==="subheader")return '<h2>A.</h2>';
if(type==="text")return '<p>Write test content here...</p>';
if(type==="gap")return '<div style="height:70px"></div>';
if(type==="image"){imageInput.click();return ""}
if(type==="audio"){audioInput.click();return ""}
if(type==="video"){videoInput.click();return ""}
return "";
}

document.querySelectorAll(".block-btn").forEach(btn=>btn.onclick=()=>{const type=btn.dataset.block;const html=template(type);if(html)addCard(html,type==="gap")});
canvas.onclick=e=>{if(e.target===canvas||e.target.classList.contains("empty-state"))selectAll()};

function read(file,cb){const r=new FileReader();r.onload=()=>cb(r.result);r.readAsDataURL(file)}
imageInput.onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)read(f,src=>addCard('<div class="media-resizer"><img src="'+src+'"></div>'));e.target.value=""};
audioInput.onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)read(f,src=>addCard('<audio src="'+src+'" controls style="width:100%"></audio>'));e.target.value=""};
videoInput.onchange=e=>{const f=e.target.files[0];if(f)read(f,src=>addCard('<div class="media-resizer"><video src="'+src+'" controls></video></div>'));e.target.value=""};

function apply(prop,val){targetCards().forEach(c=>c.style[prop]=val)}
fontFamily.onchange=e=>apply("fontFamily",e.target.value);
fontSize.onchange=e=>apply("fontSize",e.target.value);
lineSpacing.onchange=e=>apply("lineHeight",e.target.value);
alignment.onchange=e=>apply("textAlign",e.target.value);
fontColor.oninput=e=>apply("color",e.target.value);
backgroundColor.oninput=e=>apply("backgroundColor",e.target.value);
cardSize.onchange=e=>targetCards().forEach(c=>c.style.width=e.target.value);
cardAlignLeft.onclick=()=>targetCards().forEach(c=>{c.style.marginLeft="0";c.style.marginRight="auto"});
cardAlignCenter.onclick=()=>targetCards().forEach(c=>{c.style.marginLeft="auto";c.style.marginRight="auto"});
cardAlignRight.onclick=()=>targetCards().forEach(c=>{c.style.marginLeft="auto";c.style.marginRight="0"});
document.querySelectorAll("[data-toggle]").forEach(btn=>btn.onclick=()=>targetCards().forEach(c=>{if(btn.dataset.toggle==="bold")c.style.fontWeight=c.style.fontWeight==="900"?"700":"900";if(btn.dataset.toggle==="italic")c.style.fontStyle=c.style.fontStyle==="italic"?"normal":"italic";if(btn.dataset.toggle==="underline")c.style.textDecoration=c.style.textDecoration==="underline"?"none":"underline"}));

undoBtn.onclick=()=>{if(!undoStack.length)return;canvas.innerHTML=undoStack.pop();allCards().forEach(bindCard)};

async function saveTest(){
const payload={title:titleInput.value.trim()||"Untitled Placement Test",content:canvas.innerHTML,updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()};
if(currentId){await db.collection("placementTests").doc(currentId).set(payload,{merge:true})}
else{const ref=await db.collection("placementTests").add(payload);currentId=ref.id;history.replaceState(null,"","/teacher/placements/builder.html?edit="+currentId)}
tick();return currentId;
}

saveBtn.onclick=async e=>{e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();await saveTest()};
newBtn.onclick=e=>{e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();currentId="";titleInput.value="";canvas.innerHTML='<div class="empty-state">Add placement test blocks from the left. Click inside the canvas to select all blocks for formatting.</div>';history.replaceState(null,"","/teacher/placements/builder.html")};
viewBtn.onclick=async e=>{e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();const id=await saveTest();window.open("/teacher/placements/view-test.html?id="+encodeURIComponent(id),"_blank")};

async function load(){
if(!currentId)return;
const doc=await db.collection("placementTests").doc(currentId).get();
if(!doc.exists)return;
const d=doc.data();
titleInput.value=d.title||"";
canvas.innerHTML=d.content||'<div class="empty-state">Add placement test blocks from the left. Click inside the canvas to select all blocks for formatting.</div>';
allCards().forEach(bindCard);
}
load();
});
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0">
<title>Placement Recordings | Impact</title>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Sorts+Mill+Goudy&family=Inter:wght@400;600;800;900&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/impact-global-bg.css">
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/teacher/placements/placements.css">

<body>
<script src="/js/impact-global-bg.js"></script>

<nav class="lp-nav">
  <a class="lp-icon-btn" href="/teacher/dashboard.html" title="Dashboard"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><rect x="4" y="4" width="7" height="7" rx="2"/><rect x="13" y="4" width="7" height="7" rx="2"/><rect x="4" y="13" width="7" height="7" rx="2"/><rect x="13" y="13" width="7" height="7" rx="2"/></svg></a>
  <a class="lp-icon-btn" href="/teacher/placements/index.html" title="Back"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M15 5.5 8.5 12 15 18.5"/><path d="M9 12h11"/></svg></a>
</nav>

<main class="page">
  <section class="hero">
    <p class="eyebrow">Placement Audio Library</p>
    <h1>Placement Recordings</h1>
    <p>Upload learner placement recordings and organize them by level.</p>
  </section>

  <section class="two-col">
    <aside class="panel" style="padding:22px">
      <h2 style="margin-bottom:16px">Level Folders</h2>
      <div class="level-list" id="levels"></div>
    </aside>

    <section class="panel" style="padding:22px">
      <div class="upload-bar">
        <input id="file" type="file" accept="audio/*,video/*">
        <select id="folder"></select>
        <button id="uploadBtn">Upload</button>
      </div>
      <div id="recordingList"><div class="empty">Loading...</div></div>
    </section>
  </section>
</main>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-firestore-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-storage-compat.js"></script>
<script src="/__/firebase/init.js"></script>
<script>
const db=firebase.firestore();
const storage=firebase.storage();
const levels=["Absolute Beginner","A0","A1","A1.1","A2","B1","B2"];
let current=levels[0];

levels.forEach(level=>{
  const b=document.createElement("button");
  b.className="level-btn";
  b.textContent=level;
  b.onclick=()=>{current=level;paint();load();};
  document.getElementById("levels").appendChild(b);

  const o=document.createElement("option");
  o.textContent=level;
  document.getElementById("folder").appendChild(o);
});

function paint(){
  document.querySelectorAll(".level-btn").forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle("active",b.textContent===current));
  document.getElementById("folder").value=current;
}

async function upload(){
  const file=document.getElementById("file").files[0];
  if(!file)return;
  const level=document.getElementById("folder").value;
  const path=`placement-recordings/${level}/${Date.now()}-${file.name}`;
  const ref=storage.ref(path);
  await ref.put(file);
  const url=await ref.getDownloadURL();
  await db.collection("placementRecordings").add({name:file.name,level,url,type:file.type,path,createdAt:new Date().toISOString()});
  document.getElementById("file").value="";
  current=level;
  paint();
  load();
}

async function load(){
  const box=document.getElementById("recordingList");
  box.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Loading recordings...</div>';
  const snap=await db.collection("placementRecordings").where("level","==",current).get();
  box.innerHTML="";
  if(snap.empty){
    box.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No recordings in this folder yet.</div>';
    return;
  }
  snap.forEach(doc=>{
    const r=doc.data();
    const item=document.createElement("div");
    item.className="recording-item";
    item.innerHTML=`<strong>${r.name}</strong>${(r.type||"").startsWith("video")?`<video src="${r.url}" controls></video>`:`<audio src="${r.url}" controls></audio>`}`;
    box.appendChild(item);
  });
}

document.getElementById("uploadBtn").onclick=upload;
paint();
load();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

<main class="page">
  <section class="hero">
    <p class="eyebrow">Learner Reports</p>
    <h1>Placement Reports</h1>
    <p>Search and review all learner placement results in one place.</p>
  </section>

  <section class="panel" style="padding:24px">
    <input class="search" id="search" placeholder="Search by learner name, level, result, teacher, or recommendation...">
    <div id="reports"><div class="empty">Loading reports...</div></div>
  </section>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-firestore-compat.js"></script>
<script src="/__/firebase/init.js"></script>
<script>
const db=firebase.firestore();
let all=[];

function render(){
  const q=document.getElementById("search").value.toLowerCase();
  const box=document.getElementById("reports");
  const rows=all.filter(r=>JSON.stringify(r).toLowerCase().includes(q));
  box.innerHTML="";
  if(!rows.length){
    box.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No reports found.</div>';
    return;
  }
  rows.forEach(r=>{
    const item=document.createElement("article");
    item.className="report-item";
    item.innerHTML=`
      <h2>${r.learner || r.name || "Unnamed Learner"}</h2>
      <p class="soft-text">${r.level || "No level"} • ${r.result || r.placement || "No placement result"} • ${r.teacher || "No teacher"}</p>
      <p style="margin-top:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.74);font-weight:700;line-height:1.7">${r.remarks || r.report || r.recommendation || "No report details yet."}</p>
    `;
    box.appendChild(item);
  });
}

async function load(){
  const box=document.getElementById("reports");
  box.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Loading reports...</div>';
  try{
    const snap=await db.collection("placementReports").get();
    all=[];
    snap.forEach(doc=>all.push(doc.data()));
    render();
  }catch(e){
    box.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Could not load reports.</div>';
  }
}

document.getElementById("search").oninput=render;
load();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
const db=firebase.firestore();
const list=document.getElementById("testList");

document.getElementById("createBtn").onclick=function(){
  location.href="/teacher/placements/builder.html";
};

async function load(){
  list.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Loading placement tests...</div>';
  try{
    const snap=await db.collection("placementTests").orderBy("updatedAt","desc").get();
    list.innerHTML="";
    if(snap.empty){
      list.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No placement tests created yet.</div>';
      return;
    }
    snap.forEach(doc=>{
      const t=doc.data();
      const row=document.createElement("div");
      row.className="row";
      row.innerHTML=`
        <strong>${t.title || "Untitled Placement Test"}</strong>
        <a href="/teacher/placements/view-test.html?id=${doc.id}">View</a>
        <a href="/teacher/placements/builder.html?edit=${doc.id}">Edit</a>
        <button data-id="${doc.id}">Delete</button>
      `;
      row.querySelector("button").onclick=async()=>{await db.collection("placementTests").doc(doc.id).delete();load();};
      list.appendChild(row);
    });
  }catch(e){
    list.innerHTML='<div class="empty">Could not load placement tests.</div>';
  }
}
load();
</script>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>

<script>
const db=firebase.firestore();
const id=new URLSearchParams(location.search).get("id");

async function load(){
  const docBox=document.getElementById("doc");
  const titleBox=document.getElementById("pageTitle");
  const targetBox=document.getElementById("targetText");

  if(!id){
    titleBox.textContent="No test selected";
    docBox.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No placement test ID was provided.</div>';
    return;
  }

  const snap=await db.collection("placementTests").doc(id).get();

  if(!snap.exists){
    titleBox.textContent="Not found";
    docBox.innerHTML='<div class="empty">This placement test could not be found.</div>';
    return;
  }

  const test=snap.data();

  titleBox.textContent=test.title || "Untitled Placement Test";
  targetBox.textContent=test.target || "";

  if(test.content && test.content.trim()){
    docBox.innerHTML=test.content;
    docBox.querySelectorAll("[contenteditable]").forEach(el=>el.removeAttribute("contenteditable"));
    docBox.querySelectorAll(".delete-card").forEach(btn=>btn.remove());
    docBox.querySelectorAll("[contenteditable]").forEach(el=>el.removeAttribute("contenteditable"));
docBox.querySelectorAll(".delete-card").forEach(btn=>btn.remove());
docBox.querySelectorAll(".lesson-card").forEach(card=>{
  card.classList.remove("active");
  card.removeAttribute("draggable");
});
    return;
  }

  docBox.innerHTML='<div class="empty">This test has no content yet. Go back and edit the test.</div>';
}
load();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

<script id="inline-folder-create-script">
(function(){
  function patchCreateButtons(){
    document.querySelectorAll("button,a,div").forEach(btn=>{
      const text = (btn.textContent || "").trim().toLowerCase();

      if(!text.includes("create first subfolder") && !text.includes("create subfolder")) return;
      if(btn.dataset.inlineFolderPatched === "yes") return;

      btn.dataset.inlineFolderPatched = "yes";

      btn.onclick = function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();

        const parent = btn.parentElement;
        if(!parent || parent.querySelector(".inline-folder-create")) return;

        const form = document.createElement("div");
        form.className = "inline-folder-create";
        form.innerHTML = `
          <input placeholder="Subfolder name">
          <button type="button">Save</button>
        `;

        parent.appendChild(form);

        const input = form.querySelector("input");
        input.focus();

        form.querySelector("button").onclick = async function(){
          const name = input.value.trim();
          if(!name) return;

          const pill = document.createElement("div");
          pill.className = "subfolder-pill";
          pill.textContent = name;

          form.replaceWith(pill);

          try{
            if(window.firebase && firebase.firestore){
              const db = firebase.firestore();
              await db.collection("recordingSubfolders").add({
                name,
                createdAt:new Date().toISOString()
              });
            }
          }catch(err){
            console.warn("Subfolder saved visually, Firestore save skipped:", err);
          }
        };
      };
    });
  }

  setTimeout(patchCreateButtons,300);
  setTimeout(patchCreateButtons,1000);
})();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-round-icons.js?v=001"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
