<script>
const db = firebase.firestore();
const list = document.getElementById("binList");
const selected = new Set();

function label(item){
  return item.title || item.fileName || item.documentId || item.storagePath || "Deleted item";
}

function meta(item){
  const parts = [];
  if(item.type) parts.push(item.type);
  if(item.collection) parts.push("Collection: " + item.collection);
  if(item.storagePath) parts.push("Path: " + item.storagePath);
  if(item.sourceUrl) parts.push("Deleted from: " + item.sourceUrl);
  return parts.join(" • ");
}

async function loadBin(){
  selected.clear();
  document.getElementById("selectAll").checked = false;
  list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">Loading 
recycle bin...</div>';

  const snap = await db.collection("recycleBin").orderBy("deletedAt","desc").get();

  if(snap.empty){
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">
Recycle bin is empty.</div>';
    return;
  }

  list.innerHTML = "";

  snap.forEach(doc=>{
    const item = doc.data();
    const row = document.createElement("article");
    row.className = "item";
    row.innerHTML = `
      <input type="checkbox" data-id="${doc.id}">
      <div>
        <h3>${label(item)}</h3>
        <div class="meta">${item.deletedAtText || item.deletedAt || ""}</div>
        <div class="meta">${meta(item)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="row-actions">
        <button class="danger" data-delete="${doc.id}">Delete Permanently</button>
      </div>
    `;

    row.querySelector("input").onchange = e=>{
      if(e.target.checked) selected.add(doc.id);
      else selected.delete(doc.id);
    };

    row.querySelector("[data-delete]").onclick = async ()=>{
      await db.collection("recycleBin").doc(doc.id).delete();
      loadBin();
    };

    list.appendChild(row);
  });
}

document.getElementById("selectAll").onchange = e=>{
  selected.clear();
  document.querySelectorAll('#binList input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb=>{
    cb.checked = e.target.checked;
    if(cb.checked) selected.add(cb.dataset.id);
  });
};

document.getElementById("deleteSelected").onclick = async ()=>{
  if(!selected.size) return;
  const batch = db.batch();
  selected.forEach(id=>batch.delete(db.collection("recycleBin").doc(id)));
  await batch.commit();
  loadBin();
};

document.getElementById("refreshBtn").onclick = loadBin;
loadBin();
</script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>
<script id="recycle-permanent-delete-fix">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
  if(!window.firebase || !firebase.firestore) return;

  const db=firebase.firestore();

  document.addEventListener("click",async function(e){
    const btn=e.target.closest("[data-delete-permanent], .delete-permanent, .permanent-delete, button");
    if(!btn) return;

    const text=(btn.textContent||"").toLowerCase();
    if(!btn.matches("[data-delete-permanent], .delete-permanent, .permanent-delete") && !text.includes("delete permanently")) return;

    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();

    const id=btn.dataset.id || btn.dataset.deletePermanent || btn.closest("[data-id]")?.dataset.id;
    if(!id){
      alert("Could not find recycle item ID.");
      return;
    }

    if(!confirm("Delete this item permanently?")) return;

    await db.collection("recycleBin").doc(id).delete();

    const row=btn.closest(".recycle-row,.bin-row,.record,.item,article,div");
    if(row) row.remove();

    alert("Deleted permanently.");
  },true);
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-firestore-compat.js"></script>
<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-storage-compat.js"></script>
<script src="/__/firebase/init.js"></script>
<script src="/js/impact-recycle-bin.js"></script>

<script>
const db = firebase.firestore();
const storage = firebase.storage();

const docInput = document.getElementById("docInput");
const docList = document.getElementById("docList");
const searchInput = document.getElementById("searchInput");
const uploadStatus = document.getElementById("uploadStatus");
const uploaderNameEl = document.getElementById("uploaderName");

const uploader =
  sessionStorage.getItem("impactAccessName") ||
  sessionStorage.getItem("impactPersonnelName") ||
  sessionStorage.getItem("impactUserName") ||
  "User";

uploaderNameEl.textContent = uploader;

let allDocs = [];

function safeText(value){
  return String(value || "").replace(/[<>&"]/g, ch => ({
    "<":"&lt;",
    ">":"&gt;",
    "&":"&amp;",
    '"':"&quot;"
  }[ch]));
}

function formatBytes(bytes){
  if(!bytes) return "Unknown size";
  const units = ["B","KB","MB","GB"];
  let size = bytes;
  let index = 0;
  while(size >= 1024 && index < units.length - 1){
    size = size / 1024;
    index++;
  }
  return size.toFixed(index === 0 ? 0 : 1) + " " + units[index];
}

async function loadDocs(){
  docList.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">Loading documents...</div>';

  const snap = await db.collection("teamDocs").orderBy("uploadedAt","desc").get();
  allDocs = [];

  snap.forEach(doc => {
    allDocs.push({ id: doc.id, ...doc.data() });
  });

  renderDocs(allDocs);
}

function renderDocs(items){
  if(!items.length){
    docList.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No team documents found.</div>';
    return;
  }

  docList.innerHTML = "";

  items.forEach(item => {
    const row = document.createElement("article");
    row.className = "doc-row";

    row.innerHTML = `
      <div>
        <h3>${safeText(item.name || "Untitled Document")}</h3>
        <div class="meta">Uploaded by ${safeText(item.uploadedBy || "User")}</div>
        <div class="meta">${safeText(item.uploadedAtText || "")} • ${safeText(item.type || "file")} • ${safeText(formatBytes(item.size))}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="row-actions">
        <a href="${item.url}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Open</a>
        <button type="button" data-delete="${item.id}">Delete</button>
      </div>
    `;

    row.querySelector("[data-delete]").onclick = async () => {
      await deleteDocItem(item);
    };

    docList.appendChild(row);
  });
}

async function deleteDocItem(item){
  try{
    if(window.ImpactRecycleBin){
      await window.ImpactRecycleBin.send({
        type: "team-doc",
        title: item.name || "Team document",
        collection: "teamDocs",
        documentId: item.id,
        storagePath: item.storagePath || "",
        fileName: item.name || "",
        data: item
      });
    }

    await db.collection("teamDocs").doc(item.id).delete();

    if(item.storagePath){
      try{
        await storage.ref(item.storagePath).delete();
      }catch(e){
        console.warn("Storage delete skipped:", e);
      }
    }

    await loadDocs();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    alert("Could not delete this document.");
  }
}

docInput.onchange = async e => {
  const file = e.target.files[0];
  if(!file) return;

  try{
    uploadStatus.textContent = "Uploading " + file.name + "...";

    const stamp = Date.now();
    const cleanName = file.name.replace(/[^\w.\-() ]+/g, "_");
    const path = "team-docs/" + stamp + "-" + cleanName;

    const ref = storage.ref(path);
    await ref.put(file);
    const url = await ref.getDownloadURL();

    const now = new Date();

    await db.collection("teamDocs").add({
      name: file.name,
      type: file.type || "file",
      size: file.size || 0,
      url,
      storagePath: path,
      uploadedBy: uploader,
      uploadedAt: now.toISOString(),
      uploadedAtText: now.toLocaleString(),
      uploadDate: now.toLocaleDateString(),
      uploadTime: now.toLocaleTimeString(),
      extension: (file.name.split(".").pop() || "file").toLowerCase()
    });

    uploadStatus.textContent = "Uploaded successfully ✓";
    docInput.value = "";
    await loadDocs();
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    uploadStatus.textContent = "Upload failed. Please try again.";
  }
};

function runSearch(){
  const q = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();

  if(!q){
    renderDocs(allDocs);
    return;
  }

  const filtered = allDocs.filter(item => {
    const text = [
      item.name,
      item.uploadedBy,
      item.uploadedAtText,
      item.type,
      item.storagePath
    ].join(" ").toLowerCase();

    return text.includes(q);
  });

  renderDocs(filtered);
}

document.getElementById("searchBtn").onclick = runSearch;
searchInput.oninput = runSearch;

loadDocs();
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
(async function(){
  if(sessionStorage.getItem("impactTeamLeadAccess") !== "granted"){
    window.location.href = "/gate/team-lead.html";
    return;
  }

  const passkeyList = document.getElementById("passkeyList");
  const visitList = document.getElementById("visitList");

  let db = null;

  try{
    db = firebase.firestore();
  }catch(e){
    db = null;
  }

  function getLocalPasskeys(){
    try{
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactPasskeys") || "[]");
    }catch(e){
      return [];
    }
  }

  function saveLocalPasskeys(list){
    localStorage.setItem("impactPasskeys", JSON.stringify(list));
  }

  function getLocalVisits(){
    try{
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactGateVisits") || "[]");
    }catch(e){
      return [];
    }
  }

  async function migrateLocalToFirebase(){
    if(!db) return;

    const local = getLocalPasskeys();

    for(const item of local){
      if(!item.passkey) continue;

      const existing = await db.collection("impactPasskeys")
        .where("passkey","==",item.passkey)
        .limit(1)
        .get();

      if(existing.empty){
        await db.collection("impactPasskeys").add({
          name:item.name || "Unnamed",
          role:item.role || "teacher",
          passkey:item.passkey,
          status:item.status || "active",
          createdAt:item.createdAt || new Date().toISOString(),
          migratedFromLocal:true
        });
      }
    }
  }

  function renderPasskeys(rows){
    rows.sort((a,b)=>{
      const aInactive = (a.status || "active") !== "active";
      const bInactive = (b.status || "active") !== "active";

      if(aInactive && !bInactive) return 1;
      if(!aInactive && bInactive) return -1;

      return String(a.name || "").localeCompare(String(b.name || ""));
    });

    if(!rows.length){
      passkeyList.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No passkeys created yet.</div>';
      return;
    }

    passkeyList.innerHTML = rows.map(item => {
      const inactive = (item.status || "active") !== "active";

      return `
        <div class="row ${inactive ? "inactive" : ""}">
          <div>
            <strong>${item.name || "Unnamed"}</strong>
            <span>${item.role || "teacher"} • ${item.passkey || "No passkey"}</span>
            <span class="status-pill">${inactive ? "Inactive" : "Active"}</span>
          </div>
          <button data-id="${item.id}" ${inactive ? "disabled" : ""} type="button">
            ${inactive ? "Inactive" : "Deactivate"}
          </button>
        </div>
      `;
    }).join("");

    passkeyList.querySelectorAll("button[data-id]").forEach(btn => {
      btn.onclick = async function(){
        if(!confirm("Deactivate this passkey?")) return;

        if(db && btn.dataset.id.length > 10){
          await db.collection("impactPasskeys").doc(btn.dataset.id).update({
            status:"deactivated",
            deactivatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
          });
        }else{
          const list = getLocalPasskeys().map(item => {
            if(item.id === btn.dataset.id) item.status = "deactivated";
            return item;
          });
          saveLocalPasskeys(list);
          renderPasskeys(list);
        }
      };
    });
  }

  function renderVisits(rows){
    rows.sort((a,b)=>String(b.time || "").localeCompare(String(a.time || "")));

    if(!rows.length){
      visitList.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No tracked visits yet.</div>';
      return;
    }

    visitList.innerHTML = rows.map(v => `
      <div class="row visit-row">
        <div>
          <strong>${v.name || "Unknown visitor"}</strong>
          <span>${v.role || "unknown"} • ${v.gate || "unknown gate"}</span>
          <span>${v.time ? new Date(v.time).toLocaleString() : ""}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    `).join("");
  }

  if(db){
    await migrateLocalToFirebase();

    db.collection("impactPasskeys").onSnapshot(snapshot => {
      const rows = [];
      snapshot.forEach(doc => rows.push({id:doc.id, ...doc.data()}));
      renderPasskeys(rows);
    });

    db.collection("impactGateVisits").onSnapshot(snapshot => {
      const rows = [];
      snapshot.forEach(doc => rows.push({id:doc.id, ...doc.data()}));
      renderVisits(rows);
    });
  }else{
    renderPasskeys(getLocalPasskeys());
    renderVisits(getLocalVisits());
  }
})();
</script>
<script id="FORCE_PASSKEY_FIRESTORE_MIGRATION">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
  const passkeyList = document.getElementById("passkeyList");

  function showError(msg){
    passkeyList.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">${msg}</div>`;
  }

  function getLocalPasskeys(){
    const keys = [];

    try{
      const a = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impactPasskeys") || "[]");
      if(Array.isArray(a)) keys.push(...a);
    }catch(e){}

    try{
      const b = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("impact_keys") || "[]");
      if(Array.isArray(b)) keys.push(...b);
    }catch(e){}

    return keys;
  }

  function normalizeRole(role){
    const r = String(role || "Teacher").trim();
    if(r.toLowerCase() === "personnel") return "Teacher";
    return r;
  }

  function normalizeStatus(status, active){
    if(status) return String(status).toLowerCase() === "deactivated" || String(status).toLowerCase() === "inactive" ? "deactivated" : "active";
    return active === false ? "deactivated" : "active";
  }

  async function waitForFirebase(){
    for(let i=0;i<40;i++){
      if(window.firebase && firebase.apps && firebase.apps.length && firebase.firestore){
        return firebase.firestore();
      }
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r,150));
    }
    throw new Error("Firebase did not load.");
  }

  async function migrateLocalPasskeys(db){
    const local = getLocalPasskeys();

    for(const item of local){
      const passkey = item.passkey || item.key || item.code;
      if(!passkey) continue;

      const existing = await db.collection("impactPasskeys")
        .where("passkey","==",passkey)
        .limit(1)
        .get();

      if(existing.empty){
        await db.collection("impactPasskeys").add({
          name:item.name || item.fullName || item.memberName || "Unnamed",
          role:normalizeRole(item.role),
          passkey:passkey,
          status:normalizeStatus(item.status,item.active),
          createdAt:item.createdAt || new Date().toISOString(),
          migratedFromLocal:true,
          migratedAt:new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }
    }
  }

  function renderPasskeys(snapshot){
    const rows = [];
    snapshot.forEach(doc => rows.push({id:doc.id,...doc.data()}));

    rows.sort((a,b)=>{
      const ai = (a.status || "active") !== "active";
      const bi = (b.status || "active") !== "active";
      if(ai && !bi) return 1;
      if(!ai && bi) return -1;
      return String(a.name || "").localeCompare(String(b.name || ""));
    });

    if(!rows.length){
      passkeyList.innerHTML = `<div class="empty">No passkeys created yet.</div>`;
      return;
    }

    passkeyList.innerHTML = rows.map(item => {
      const inactive = (item.status || "active") !== "active";
      return `
        <div class="row ${inactive ? "inactive" : ""}">
          <div>
            <strong>${item.name || "Unnamed"}</strong>
            <span>${item.role || "Teacher"} • ${item.passkey || "No passkey"}</span>
            <span class="status-pill">${inactive ? "Inactive" : "Active"}</span>
          </div>
          <button data-id="${item.id}" ${inactive ? "disabled" : ""} type="button">
            ${inactive ? "Inactive" : "Deactivate"}
          </button>
        </div>
      `;
    }).join("");

    passkeyList.querySelectorAll("button[data-id]").forEach(btn => {
      btn.onclick = async () => {
        if(!confirm("Deactivate this passkey?")) return;
        const db = firebase.firestore();
        await db.collection("impactPasskeys").doc(btn.dataset.id).update({
          status:"deactivated",
          deactivatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
        });
      };
    });
  }

  try{
    const db = await waitForFirebase();

    await migrateLocalPasskeys(db);

    db.collection("impactPasskeys").onSnapshot(renderPasskeys, err => {
      showError("Firestore read failed: " + err.message);
    });

  }catch(err){
    showError("Could not load Firestore: " + err.message);
  }
});
</script>

<script src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.4/firebase-app-compat.js"></script>

<script>
const db=firebase.firestore();
const link=document.getElementById("meetingLink");
const minutes=document.getElementById("meetingMinutes");
const btn=document.getElementById("meetingBtn");
const statusBox=document.getElementById("meetingStatus");
const records=document.getElementById("records");

let active=null;

function person(){
  return sessionStorage.getItem("impactAccessName") ||
         sessionStorage.getItem("impactPersonnelName") ||
         "User";
}

async function load(){
  const snap=await db.collection("teamMeetings").orderBy("startedAt","desc").get();
  const list=snap.docs.map(d=>({id:d.id,...d.data()}));

  if(!list.length){
    records.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No team meeting records yet.</div>';
    return;
  }

  records.innerHTML="";
  list.forEach(item=>{
    const div=document.createElement("div");
    div.className="record";
    div.innerHTML=`
      <h3>${item.title || "Team Meeting"}</h3>
      <div class="meta">Started by ${item.startedBy || ""}</div>
      <div class="meta">Started: ${item.startedAtText || ""}</div>
      <div class="meta">Ended: ${item.endedAtText || "Still running / not ended"}</div>
      <div class="meta">Duration: ${item.minutesSpent || 0} minute(s)</div>
      <div class="meta">Link: ${item.meetingLink || ""}</div>
      <div class="meta">Minutes: ${item.minutes || ""}</div>
    `;
    records.appendChild(div);
  });
}

btn.onclick=async()=>{
  if(!active){
    const startedAt=new Date();
    const ref=await db.collection("teamMeetings").add({
      title:"Team Meeting",
      meetingLink:link.value.trim(),
      minutes:minutes.value.trim(),
      startedBy:person(),
      startedAt:startedAt.toISOString(),
      startedAtText:startedAt.toLocaleString(),
      endedAt:"",
      endedAtText:"",
      minutesSpent:0,
      status:"Started"
    });

    active={id:ref.id,startedAt};
    window.open(link.value.trim(),"_blank");
    btn.textContent="End Meeting";
    statusBox.textContent="Meeting started ✓";
    await load();
    return;
  }

  const endedAt=new Date();
  const minutesSpent=Math.round((endedAt-active.startedAt)/60000);

  await db.collection("teamMeetings").doc(active.id).set({
    minutes:minutes.value.trim(),
    endedAt:endedAt.toISOString(),
    endedAtText:endedAt.toLocaleString(),
    minutesSpent,
    status:"Ended"
  },{merge:true});

  active=null;
  btn.textContent="Start Meeting";
  statusBox.textContent="Meeting ended and logged ✓";
  await load();
};

load();
</script>
</body>
</html>

FILE: safe-backups\20260426-225842\activities.js

import {
  collection,
  addDoc,
  getDocs,
  query,
  orderBy,
  serverTimestamp
} from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.0/firebase-firestore.js";

import { db } from "/js/firebase-app.js";

const STORAGE_KEYS = {
  folders: "impactActivityFolders",
  activities: "impactActivities"
};

let folders = [];
let activities = [];
let selectedFolderId = "all";
let fields = [];

const $ = (id) => document.getElementById(id);

function toast(message){
  const box = $("toast");
  if(!box) return;
  box.textContent = message;
  box.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => box.classList.remove("show"), 2200);
}

function escapeHtml(value){
  return String(value || "")
    .replaceAll("&","&amp;").replaceAll("<","&lt;").replaceAll(">","&gt;")
    .replaceAll('"',"&quot;").replaceAll("'","&#039;");
}

function localRead(key){
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || "[]"); }
  catch { return []; }
}

function localWrite(key, data){
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(data));
}

function docDate(value){
  if(!value) return new Date().toLocaleString();
  if(value.toDate) return value.toDate().toLocaleString();
  if(value.seconds) return new Date(value.seconds * 1000).toLocaleString();
  return String(value);
}

function fieldId(){
  return "field_" + Date.now() + "_" + Math.random().toString(16).slice(2);
}

async function loadFolders(){
  try{
    const snap = await getDocs(query(collection(db, "activityFolders"), orderBy("createdAt", "desc")));
    folders = [];
    snap.forEach((doc) => folders.push({ id: doc.id, ...doc.data() }));
    localWrite(STORAGE_KEYS.folders, folders);
  }catch(err){
    folders = localRead(STORAGE_KEYS.folders);
  }
}

async function loadActivities(){
  try{
    const snap = await getDocs(query(collection(db, "activities"), orderBy("createdAt", "desc")));
    activities = [];
    snap.forEach((doc) => activities.push({ id: doc.id, ...doc.data() }));
    localWrite(STORAGE_KEYS.activities, activities);
  }catch(err){
    activities = localRead(STORAGE_KEYS.activities);
  }
}

function renderFolderOptions(){
  const select = $("activityFolder");
  select.innerHTML = `<option value="">Select Folder</option>` + folders.map(folder =>
    `<option value="${folder.id}">${escapeHtml(folder.name)}</option>`
  ).join("");
}

function renderFolders(){
  $("folderCount").textContent = folders.length;

  const allCount = activities.length;
  $("folderList").innerHTML = `
    <button class="activity-folder ${selectedFolderId === "all" ? "active" : ""}" data-id="all" data-name="All Activities" type="button">
      <span class="folder-icon"></span>
      <div><strong>All Activities</strong><small>${allCount} activities</small></div>
    </button>
    ${folders.map(folder => {
      const count = activities.filter(item => item.folderId === folder.id).length;
      return `
        <button class="activity-folder ${selectedFolderId === folder.id ? "active" : ""}" data-id="${folder.id}" data-name="${escapeHtml(folder.name)}" type="button">
          <span class="folder-icon"></span>
          <div><strong>${escapeHtml(folder.name)}</strong><small>${count} activities</small></div>
        </button>
      `;
    }).join("")}
  `;

  document.querySelectorAll(".activity-folder").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      selectedFolderId = btn.dataset.id;
      $("selectedFolderTitle").textContent = btn.dataset.name;
      renderFolders();
      renderActivities();
    });
  });

  renderFolderOptions();
}

function renderActivities(){
  const visible = selectedFolderId === "all"
    ? activities
    : activities.filter(item => item.folderId === selectedFolderId);

  $("activityCount").textContent = `${visible.length} ${visible.length === 1 ? "activity" : "activities"}`;

  if(!visible.length){
    $("activityList").innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">No activity saved in this folder yet.</div>`;
    return;
  }

  $("activityList").innerHTML = visible.map(item => `
    <article class="activity-card">
      <div class="activity-card-top">
        <div>
          <p>${escapeHtml(item.type || "Activity")}</p>
          <h3>${escapeHtml(item.title || "Untitled Activity")}</h3>
        </div>
        <span class="status-pill">${escapeHtml(item.status || "Created")}</span>
      </div>
      <p class="activity-note">
        ${escapeHtml(item.level || "Level not set")} �
        ${escapeHtml(item.personnel || "personnel not set")} �
        ${escapeHtml(item.impactLearnersGroup || "impactLearners/group not set")} �
        ${item.fields?.length || 0} blocks
      </p>
      <p class="activity-note">${escapeHtml(item.instructions || "No instructions added.")}</p>
    </article>
  `).join("");
}

function renderTracker(){
  const created = activities.filter(a => a.status === "Created").length;
  const published = activities.filter(a => a.status === "Published").length;
  const completed = activities.filter(a => a.status === "Completed").length;

  $("createdCount").textContent = created;
  $("publishedCount").textContent = published;
  $("completedCount").textContent = completed;
  $("trackerCount").textContent = `${activities.length} records`;

  if(!activities.length){
    $("trackerList").innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">No activity records yet.</div>`;
    return;
  }

  $("trackerList").innerHTML = activities.map(item => {
    const folder = folders.find(f => f.id === item.folderId);
    return `
      <article class="tracker-row">
        <div>
          <p>${escapeHtml(item.status || "Created")} � ${escapeHtml(item.type || "Activity")}</p>
          <h3>${escapeHtml(item.title || "Untitled Activity")}</h3>
          <small>${escapeHtml(folder?.name || "No folder")} � ${escapeHtml(item.level || "No level")}</small>
        </div>
        <div>
          <strong>${docDate(item.createdAt)}</strong>
          <small>Created timestamp</small>
        </div>
      </article>
    `;
  }).join("");
}

function renderCanvas(){
  const canvas = $("canvasList");

  if(!fields.length){
    canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state">Add blocks from the left to build the activity.</div>`;
    return;
  }

  canvas.innerHTML = fields.map((field, index) => `
    <article class="field-card" data-id="${field.id}">
      <div class="field-top">
        <strong>${index + 1}. ${escapeHtml(field.type)}</strong>
        <div class="field-actions">
          <button type="button" data-up="${field.id}">?</button>
          <button type="button" data-down="${field.id}">?</button>
          <button type="button" data-remove="${field.id}">Remove</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <label>Question / Prompt
        <input data-field-label="${field.id}" type="text" value="${escapeHtml(field.label)}">
      </label>
      ${(field.type === "Multiple Choice" || field.type === "Checkboxes" || field.type === "Dropdown") ? `
        <label>Options
          <textarea data-field-options="${field.id}" rows="3">${escapeHtml((field.options || []).join("\n"))}</textarea>
        </label>
      ` : ""}
      <label>
        <select data-field-required="${field.id}">
          <option value="false" ${!field.required ? "selected" : ""}>Optional</option>
          <option value="true" ${field.required ? "selected" : ""}>Required</option>
        </select>
      </label>
    </article>
  `).join("");

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-field-label]").forEach(input => {
    input.addEventListener("input", () => {
      const field = fields.find(f => f.id === input.dataset.fieldLabel);
      if(field) field.label = input.value;
    });
  });

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-field-options]").forEach(input => {
    input.addEventListener("input", () => {
      const field = fields.find(f => f.id === input.dataset.fieldOptions);
      if(field) field.options = input.value.split("\n").map(v => v.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    });
  });

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-field-required]").forEach(input => {
    input.addEventListener("change", () => {
      const field = fields.find(f => f.id === input.dataset.fieldRequired);
      if(field) field.required = input.value === "true";
    });
  });

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-remove]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      fields = fields.filter(f => f.id !== btn.dataset.remove);
      renderCanvas();
    });
  });

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-up]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => moveField(btn.dataset.up, -1));
  });

  canvas.querySelectorAll("[data-down]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => moveField(btn.dataset.down, 1));
  });
}

function moveField(id, direction){
  const index = fields.findIndex(f => f.id === id);
  const next = index + direction;
  if(index < 0 || next < 0 || next >= fields.length) return;
  [fields[index], fields[next]] = [fields[next], fields[index]];
  renderCanvas();
}

function addField(type){
  fields.push({
    id: fieldId(),
    type,
    label: `${type} prompt`,
    required: false,
    options: type === "Multiple Choice" || type === "Checkboxes" || type === "Dropdown"
      ? ["Option 1", "Option 2"]
      : []
  });
  renderCanvas();
}

async function saveFolder(){
  const name = $("folderName").value.trim();
  if(!name){
    toast("Please enter a folder name.");
    return;
  }

  const payload = { name, createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() };

  try{
    const ref = await addDoc(collection(db, "activityFolders"), {
      name,
      createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
      updatedAt: serverTimestamp()
    });
    folders.unshift({ id: ref.id, ...payload });
  }catch(err){
    folders.unshift({ id: "local_" + Date.now(), ...payload });
  }

  localWrite(STORAGE_KEYS.folders, folders);
  $("folderName").value = "";
  closeModal("folderModal");
  renderFolders();
  toast("Folder saved.");
}

async function saveActivity(){
  const title = $("activityTitle").value.trim();
  const folderId = $("activityFolder").value;
  const level = $("activityLevel").value;

  if(!title || !folderId || !level){
    toast("Please add title, folder, and level.");
    return;
  }

  if(!fields.length){
    toast("Please add at least one form block.");
    return;
  }

  const payload = {
    type: "Activity Form",
    title,
    folderId,
    level,
    personnel: $("activitypersonnel").value.trim(),
    impactLearnersGroup: $("activityimpactLearners").value.trim(),
    status: $("activityStatus").value || "Created",
    instructions: $("activityInstructions").value.trim(),
    fields: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(fields)),
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };

  try{
    const ref = await addDoc(collection(db, "activities"), {
      ...payload,
      createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
      updatedAt: serverTimestamp()
    });
    activities.unshift({ id: ref.id, ...payload });
  }catch(err){
    activities.unshift({ id: "local_" + Date.now(), ...payload });
  }

  localWrite(STORAGE_KEYS.activities, activities);
  clearBuilder();
  closeModal("builderModal");
  renderFolders();
  renderActivities();
  renderTracker();
  toast("Activity saved.");
}

function clearBuilder(){
  ["activityTitle","activitypersonnel","activityimpactLearners","activityInstructions"].forEach(id => $(id).value = "");
  $("activityFolder").value = "";
  $("activityLevel").value = "";
  $("activityStatus").value = "Created";
  fields = [];
  renderCanvas();
}

function openModal(id){ $(id).classList.remove("hidden"); }
function closeModal(id){ $(id).classList.add("hidden"); }

function bind(){
  $("backBtn").addEventListener("click", () => history.back());
  $("openFolderBtn").addEventListener("click", () => openModal("folderModal"));
  $("openBuilderBtn").addEventListener("click", () => openModal("builderModal"));
  $("openTrackerBtn").addEventListener("click", () => { renderTracker(); openModal("trackerModal"); });
  $("saveFolderBtn").addEventListener("click", saveFolder);
  $("saveActivityBtn").addEventListener("click", saveActivity);

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-close]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => closeModal(btn.dataset.close));
  });

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-add]").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => addField(btn.dataset.add));
  });
}

async function init(){
  bind();
  await loadFolders();
  await loadActivities();
  renderFolders();
  renderActivities();
  renderTracker();
  renderCanvas();
}

init();

FILE: safe-backups\20260426-225842\lessons.js
============================================================

import {
  collection,
  addDoc,
  getDocs
} from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.0/firebase-firestore.js";

import { db } from "/js/firebase-app.js";

let folders = [];
let lessons = [];
let builder = [];

async function load(){
  let f = await getDocs(collection(db,"lessonFolders"));
  f.forEach(d=>folders.push({id:d.id,...d.data()}));

  let l = await getDocs(collection(db,"lessons"));
  l.forEach(d=>lessons.push({id:d.id,...d.data()}));

  render();
}

function render(){
  document.getElementById("folders").innerHTML =
    folders.map(f=>`<div>${f.name}</div>`).join("");

  document.getElementById("lessons").innerHTML =
    lessons.map(l=>`<div>${l.title}</div>`).join("");
}

window.openFolder = async function(){
  let name = prompt("Folder name");
  if(!name) return;

  await addDoc(collection(db,"lessonFolders"),{
    name
  });

  location.reload();
}

window.openBuilder = function(){
  let title = prompt("Lesson Title");

  let content = prompt("Lesson Content / Steps");

  let resource = prompt("Add Resource (link or text)");

  addDoc(collection(db,"lessons"),{
    title,
    content,
    resource,
    personnel:"assigned",
    impactimpactLearnerss:"group",
    createdAt:new Date().toISOString()
  });

  alert("Lesson created");
}

window.openTracker = function(){
  alert("Total Lessons: " + lessons.length);
}

load();



============================================================
FILE: seed-passkeys.js
============================================================

const admin = require("firebase-admin");

const projectId = process.env.NEW_PROJECT_ID;

const app = admin.initializeApp({
  projectId,
  credential: admin.credential.applicationDefault()
});

const db = app.firestore();

const passkeys = [
  { name:"Emelia", role:"Impact Team lead", passkey:"IMP-ZXJ$453-AM", status:"active" },
  { name:"Adelaide", role:"Academic Team lead", passkey:"IMP-HYX$862-EH", status:"active" },
  { name:"Theodosia", role:"Teacher", passkey:"IMP-VGJ$447-RS", status:"active" },
  { name:"Prosper", role:"Teacher", passkey:"IMP-YPW$392-HZ", status:"active" }
];

async function seed(){
  for(const item of passkeys){
    const existing = await db.collection("impactPasskeys")
      .where("passkey","==",item.passkey)
      .limit(1)
      .get();

    if(existing.empty){
      await db.collection("impactPasskeys").add({
        ...item,
        createdAt:new Date().toISOString(),
        source:"required_seed"
      });
      console.log("Added:", item.name);
    }else{
      await existing.docs[0].ref.set({
        ...item,
        updatedAt:new Date().toISOString()
      }, { merge:true });
      console.log("Updated:", item.name);
    }
  }

  console.log("Passkey seed complete.");
}

seed()
  .then(()=>process.exit(0))
  .catch(err=>{
    console.error(err);
    process.exit(1);
  });

rules_version = '2';

service firebase.storage {
  match /b/{bucket}/o {
    match /{allPaths=**} {
      allow read, write: if true;
    }
  }
}
